{LalVis, 5}
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvastāṃ mahatīṃ devaparṣadamanayā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya kṣamāpayitvā maṅgalyāṃ devaparṣadamāmantrayate sma gamiṣyāmyahaṃ mārṣā jambudvīpam | [LalVis, 5 1.1]
mayā pūrvabodhisattvacaryāṃ caratā sattvāścaturbhiḥ saṃgrahavastubhirnimantritā dānena priyavadyenārthakriyayā samānārthatayā ca | [LalVis, 5 1.2]
tadayuktametanmārṣā mama bhavedakṛtajñatā ca yadahamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau nābhisaṃbuddheyam | [LalVis, 5 1.3]
atha te tuṣitakāyikā devaputrā rudanto bodhisattvasya caraṇau parigṛhyaivamāhur idaṃ khalu satpuruṣa tuṣitabhavanaṃ tvayā vihīnaṃ na bhrājiṣyate | [LalVis, 5 2.1]
atha bodhisattvastāṃ mahatīṃ devaparṣadamevamāha ayaṃ maitreyo bodhisattvo yuṣmākaṃ dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati | [LalVis, 5 2.2]
atha bodhisattvaḥ svakācchirasaḥ paṭṭamaulaṃ cāvatārya maitreyasya bodhisattvasya śirasi pratiṣṭhāpayāmāsa | [LalVis, 5 2.3]
evaṃ cāvocan mamāntareṇa tvaṃ satpuruṣa anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyase | [LalVis, 5 2.4]
atha bodhisattvo maitreyaṃ bodhisattvaṃ tuṣitabhavane 'bhiniṣadya punarapi tāṃ mahatīṃ devaparṣadamāmantrayate sma kīdṛśenāhaṃ mārṣā rūpeṇa mātuḥ kukṣāvavakrāmeyaṃ tatra kecidāhur mārṣā mānavakarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.1]
kecidāhuḥ śakrarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.2]
kecidāhur brahmarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.3]
kecidāhur mahārājikarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.4]
kecidāhur vaiśravaṇarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.5]
kecidāhur gandharvarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.6]
kecidāhuḥ kinnararūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.7]
kecidāhur mahoragarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.8]
kecidāhur maheśvararūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.9]
kecidāhuś candrarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.10]
kecidāhuḥ sūryarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.11]
kecidāhur garuḍarūpeṇa | [LalVis, 5 3.12]
tatrogratejo nāma brahmakāyiko devaputraḥ pūrvarṣijanmacyuto 'vaivartiko 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ sa evamāha yathā brāhmaṇānāṃ mantravedaśāstrapāṭheṣvāgacchati tādṛśenaiva rūpeṇa bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣāvavakrāmitavyaḥ | [LalVis, 5 3.13]
tatpunaḥ kīdṛśaṃ gajavaramahāpramāṇaḥ ṣaḍdanto hemajālasaṃkāśaḥ suruciraḥ suraktaśīrṣaḥ sphuṭitagalitarūpavān | [LalVis, 5 3.14]
etacchrutvā rūpaṃ brāhmaṇavedaśāstratattvajño vyākarṣitaśca | [LalVis, 5 3.15]
ito vai bhāvī dvātriṃśallakṣaṇopetaḥ | [LalVis, 5 3.16]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo janmakālamavalokya tuṣitavarabhavanastha evaṃ rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhavare aṣṭau pūrvanimittānyupadarśayati sma | [LalVis, 5 4.1]
katamānyaṣṭau tadyathā vyapagatatṛṇakhāṇukaṇṭakaśarkarakaḍhalyanirmalaṃ suṣiktaṃ suśodhitam anākulavātatamorajovigatadaṃśakamakṣikāpataṅgasarīsṛpāpagatam avakīrṇakusumaṃ samaṃ pāṇitalajātaṃ tadgṛhaṃ saṃsthitamabhūt | [LalVis, 5 4.2]
idaṃ prathamaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 4.3]
ye ca himavatparvatarājanivāsinaḥ patraguptaśukasārikākokilahaṃsakroñcamayūracakravākakuṇālakalaviṅkajīvaṃjīvakādayo vicitrarucirapakṣā manojñapriyabhāṣiṇaḥ śakunigaṇāḥ te āgatya rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhavare vitardiniryūhatoraṇagavākṣaharmyakūṭāgāraprāsādataleṣu sthitvā pramuditāḥ prītisaumanasyajātāḥ svakasvakāni rutānyudāharanti sma | [LalVis, 5 5.1]
iti dvitīyaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 5.2]
ye ca rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyārāmaramaṇīyeṣu vanaramaṇīyeṣu codyānaramaṇīyeṣu nānāpuṣpaphalavṛkṣā nānartukārikāḥ te sarve saṃpuṣpitāḥ saṃkusumitā abhūvan | [LalVis, 5 6.1]
idaṃ tṛtīyaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 6.2]
yāśca rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya puṣkariṇyo jalaparibhogyasthāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ śakaṭacakrapramāṇairanekakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrapatraiḥ padmaiḥ saṃchāditā abhūvan | [LalVis, 5 7.1]
idaṃ caturthaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 7.2]
ye ca rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhavare bhājanaviṣaye sarpistailamadhuphāṇitaśarkarādyānāṃ te paribhujyamānāḥ kṣayaṃ na gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 5 8.1]
paripūrṇā eva saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 5 8.2]
idaṃ pañcamaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 8.3]
ye ca rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhavarapradhāne mahatyantaḥpure bherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavatūṇavavīṇāveṇuvallakīsaṃpatāḍaprabhṛtayas tūryabhāṇḍāḥ te sarve svayamaghaṭṭitā eva manojñaśabdaṃ muñcanti sma | [LalVis, 5 9.1]
idaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 9.2]
yāni ca rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhavarapradhāne suvarṇarūpyamaṇimuktāvaiḍūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālādīnāṃ ratnānāṃ bhājanāni tāni sarvāṇi niravaśeṣaṃ vivṛtavimalaviśuddhaparipūrṇānyevaṃ virocante sma | [LalVis, 5 10.1]
idaṃ saptamaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 10.2]
vimalaviśuddhayā candrasūryajihmīkaraṇayā prabhayā kāyacittodbilyasaṃjananyā tadgṛhaṃ samantādavabhāsitamabhūt | [LalVis, 5 11.1]
idamaṣṭamaṃ pūrvanimittaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 5 11.2]
māyā ca devī snātānuliptagātrā vividhābharaṇaviṣkambhitabhujā suślakṣṇasulīlavastravaradhāriṇī prītiprāmodyaprasādapratilabdhā sārdhaṃ daśabhiḥ strīsahasraiḥ parivṛtā puraskṛtā rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya saṃgītiprāsāde sukhopaviṣṭasyāntikamupasaṃkramya dakṣiṇe pārśve ratnajālapratyupte bhadrāsane niṣadya smitamukhī vyapagatabhṛkuṭikā prahasitavadanā rājānaṃ śuddhodanamābhirgāthābhirabhāṣat | [LalVis, 5 12.1]
sādho śṛṇuṣva mama pārthiva bhūmipālā yācāmi te nṛpatiradya varaṃ prayaccha | [LalVis, 5 12.2]
abhiprāyu mahya yatha cittamanaḥpraharṣaṃ tanme śṛṇuṣva bhava prītamanā udagraḥ | [LalVis, 5 12.3]
atha khalu bhikṣavaścatvāro mahārājānaḥ śakraśca devānāmindraḥ suyāmaśca devaputraḥ saṃtuṣitaśca sunirmitaśca paranirmitavaśavartī ca sārthavāhaśca māraputrabrahmā ca sahāṃpatirbrahmottaraśca purohitaḥ subrahmā ca purohitaḥ prabhāvyūhābhāsvaraśca maheśvaraśca śuddhāvāsakāyikā niṣṭhāgataścākaniṣṭhaśca etāni cānyāni cānekāni devaśatasahasrāṇi saṃnipatya anyonyamevāhur ayuktametanmārṣā asmākaṃ syādakṛtajñatā ca yadvayamekākinamadvitīyaṃ bodhisattvamutsṛjema | [LalVis, 5 27.1]
ko 'smākaṃ mārṣā utsahate bodhisattvaṃ satatasamitam anubaddhum avakramaṇagarbhasthānajanmayauvanabhūmidārakakrīḍāntaḥpuranāṭakasaṃdarśanābhiniṣkramaṇaduṣkaracaryābodhimaṇḍopasaṃkramaṇamāradharṣaṇabodhyabhisaṃbodhanadharmacakrapravartanaṃ yāvanmahāparinirvāṇāddhitacittatayā snigdhacittatayā priyacittatayā maitracittatayā saumyacittatayā tasyāṃ velāyāmimāṃ gāthāmabhāṣata | [LalVis, 5 27.2]
ko votsaheta vararūpadharam anubandhayituṃ satataṃ prītamanāḥ | [LalVis, 5 27.3]
kaḥ puṇyateja yaśasā vacasā svayamātmanecchati vibaddhayitum | [LalVis, 5 27.4]
atha khalu bhikṣavo bodhisattvasya cyavanakālasamaye pūrvasyā diśo bahūni bodhisattvaśatasahasrāṇi sarva ekajātipratibaddhāstuṣitavarabhavanavāsino yena bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāman bodhisattvasya pūjākarmaṇe | [LalVis, 5 75.1]
evaṃ daśabhyo digbhya ekaikasyā diśo bahūni bodhisattvaśatasahasrāṇi sarva ekajātipratibaddhāstuṣitavarabhavanavāsino yena bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāman bodhisattvasya pūjākarmaṇe | [LalVis, 5 75.2]
cāturmahārājakāyikebhyo devebhyaścaturaśītyapsaraḥśatasahasrāṇyevaṃ trayatriṃśato yāmebhyastuṣitebhyo nirmāṇaratibhyaḥ paranirmitavaśavartibhyo devebhyaścaturaśītyapsaraḥśatasahasrāṇi nānātūryasaṃgītivāditena yena bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāman bodhisattvasya pūjākarmaṇe | [LalVis, 5 75.3]
atha khalu bodhisattvaḥ śrīgarbhasiṃhāsane sarvapuṇyasamudgate sarvadevanāgasaṃdarśane mahākūṭāgāre niṣadya sārdhaṃ bodhisattvairdevanāgayakṣakoṭiniyutaśatasahasraiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛtastuṣitavarabhavanāt pracalati sma | [LalVis, 5 76.1]
pracalatā ca bhikṣavo bodhisattvena tathārūpā kāyāt prabhā muktābhūd yayā prabhayā ayaṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhāturevaṃ vipulavistīrṇo mahatodāreṇa supracalitapūrveṇa divyaprabhāsamatikrāntenāvabhāsena parisphuṭo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 5 76.2]
yā api tā lokāntarikā aghā aghasphuṭā andhakārāstamisrā yatremau candrasūryāvevaṃ maharddhikāvevaṃ mahānubhāvāvevaṃ maheśākhyau ābhayā ābhāṃ varṇena varṇaṃ tejasā tejo nābhitapato nābhivirocataḥ tatra ye sattvā upapannāste svakānapi bāhuprasāritānna paśyanti | [LalVis, 5 76.3]
tathāpi tasmin samaye mahata udārasyāvabhāsasya prādurbhāvo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 5 76.4]
ye ca tatra sattvā upapannāste tenaivāvabhāsena sphuṭāḥ samānā anyonyaṃ samyak paśyanti sma | [LalVis, 5 76.5]
anyonyaṃ saṃjānante sma | [LalVis, 5 76.6]
evaṃ cāhur anye 'pi kila bhoḥ sattvā ihopapannāḥ kila bho iti | [LalVis, 5 76.7]
ayaṃ ca trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhātuḥ ṣaḍvikāram aṣṭādaśamahānimittamabhūt | [LalVis, 5 77.1]
akampat prākampat samprākampat | [LalVis, 5 77.2]
avedhat prāvedhat saṃprāvedhat | [LalVis, 5 77.3]
acalat prācalat saṃprācalat | [LalVis, 5 77.4]
akṣubhyat prākṣubhyat samprākṣubhyat | [LalVis, 5 77.5]
araṇat prāraṇat saṃprāraṇat | [LalVis, 5 77.6]
agarjat prāgarjat saṃprāgarjat | [LalVis, 5 77.7]
ante 'vanamati sma madhye unnamati sma | [LalVis, 5 77.8]
madhye 'vanamati sma ante unnamati sma | [LalVis, 5 77.9]
pūrvasyāṃ diśyavanamati sma paścimāyāṃ diśyunnamati sma | [LalVis, 5 77.10]
paścimāyāṃ diśyavanamati sma pūrvasyāṃ diśyunnamati sma | [LalVis, 5 77.11]
dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśyavanamati sma uttarasyāṃ diśyunnamati sma | [LalVis, 5 77.12]
uttarasyāṃ diśyavanamati sma dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśyunnamati sma | [LalVis, 5 77.13]
tasmin samaye harṣaṇīyās toṣaṇīyāḥ premaṇīyāḥ prasādanīyā avalokanīyāḥ prahlādanīyā nirvarṇanīyā asecanīyā apratikūlā anuttrāsakarāḥ śabdāḥ śrūyante sma | [LalVis, 5 77.14]
na ca kasyacit sattvasya tasmin kṣaṇe viheṭhā vā trāso vā bhayaṃ vā stambhitatvaṃ vābhūt | [LalVis, 5 77.15]
na ca bhūyaḥ sūryācandramasorna brahmaśakralokapālānāṃ tasmin kṣaṇe prabhā prajñāyate sma | [LalVis, 5 77.16]
sarvanarakatiryagyoniyamalokopapannāśca sattvāstasmin kṣaṇe vigataduḥkhā abhūvan sarvasukhasamarpitāḥ | [LalVis, 5 77.17]
na ca kasyacit sattvasya rāgo bādhate sma dveṣo vā moho vā īrṣyā vā mātsaryaṃ vā māno vā mrakṣo vā mado vā krodho vā vyāpādo vā paridāho vā | [LalVis, 5 77.18]
sarvasattvāstasmin kṣaṇe maitracittā hitacittāḥ parasparaṃ mātāpitṛsaṅgino 'bhūvan | [LalVis, 5 77.19]
aghaṭṭitāni ca divyamānuṣyakāṇi tūryakoṭiniyutaśatasahasrāṇi manojñaghoṣamutsṛjanti sma | [LalVis, 5 77.20]
devakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi pāṇibhiraṃsaiḥ śirobhistaṃ mahāvimānaṃ vahanti sma | [LalVis, 5 77.21]
tāni cāpsaraḥśatasahasrāṇi svāṃ svāṃ saṃgītiṃ samprayujya purataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāmadakṣiṇena ca sthitvā bodhisattvaṃ saṃgītirutasvareṇābhistuvanti sma | [LalVis, 5 77.22]
pūrvakarmaśubhasaṃcitasya te dīrgharātrakuśaloditasya te | [LalVis, 5 77.23]
satyadharmanayaśodhitasya te pūja adya vipulā pravartate | [LalVis, 5 77.24]
{LalVis, 6}
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ śiśirakālavinirgate vaiśākhamāse viśākhānakṣatrānugate ṛtupravare vasantakālasamaye taruvarapatrākīrṇe varapravarapuṣpasaṃkusumite śītoṣṇatamorajovigate mṛduśādvale susaṃsthite tribhuvanajyeṣṭho lokamahito vyavalokya ṛtukālasamaye pañcadaśyāṃ pūrṇamāsyāṃ poṣadhagṛhītāyā mātuḥ puṣyanakṣatrayogena bodhisattvastuṣitavarabhavanāccyutvā smṛtaḥ samprajānan pāṇḍuro gajapoto bhūtvā ṣaḍdanta indragopakaśirāḥ suvarṇarājīdantaḥ sarvāṅgapratyaṅgo 'hīnendriyo jananyā dakṣiṇāyāṃ kukṣāvavakrāmat | [LalVis, 6 1.1]
avakrāntaśca sa dakṣiṇāvacaro 'bhūnna jātu vāmāvacaraḥ | [LalVis, 6 1.2]
māyādevī sukhaśayanaprasuptā imaṃ svapnamapaśyat | [LalVis, 6 1.3]
atha khalu māyādevī ābharaṇavigalitavasanā prahlāditakāyacittā prītiprāmodyaprasādapratilabdhā śayanavaratalādutthāya nārīgaṇaparivṛtā puraskṛtā prāsādavaraśikharādavatīrya yenāśokavanikā tenopajagāma | [LalVis, 6 4.1]
sā aśokavanikāyāṃ sukhopaviṣṭā rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya dūtaṃ preṣayati sma āgacchatu devo devī te draṣṭukāmeti | [LalVis, 6 4.2]
atha sa rājā śuddhodanastadvacanaṃ śrutvā praharṣitamanā ākampitaśarīro bhadrāsanādutthāya amātyanaigamapārṣadyabandhujanaparivṛto yenāśokavanikā tenopasaṃkrāmad upasaṃkrāntaśca na śaknoti sma aśokavanikāṃ praveṣṭum | [LalVis, 6 5.1]
gurutaramivātmānaṃ manyate sma | [LalVis, 6 5.2]
aśokavanikādvāre sthito muhūrtaṃ saṃcintya tasyāṃ velāyāmimāṃ gāthāmabhāṣata | [LalVis, 6 5.3]
vyākaritva giraṃ saumyāṃ bhuktvā pārthivabhojanam | [LalVis, 6 19.1]
ācchādanāni codgṛhya prakrāntā brāhmaṇāstataḥ | [LalVis, 6 19.2]
iti hi bhikṣavo rājā śuddhodano brāhmaṇebhyo lakṣaṇanaimittikavaipañcakebhyaḥ svapnādhyāyīpāṭhakebhyaḥ pratiśrutya hṛṣṭastuṣṭa udagra āttamanāḥ pramuditaḥ prītisaumanasyajātastān brāhmaṇān prabhūtena khādanīyabhojanīyāsvādanīyena saṃtarpya saṃpravāryācchādanāni ca dattvā visarjayati sma | [LalVis, 6 20.1]
tasyāṃ velāyāṃ kapilavastuni mahānagare caturṣu nagaradvāreṣu sarvanagaracatvaraśṛṅgāṭakeṣu ca dānaṃ dāpayati sma annamannārthikebhyaḥ pānaṃ pānārthikebhyaḥ vastrāṇi vastrārthikebhyaḥ yānāni yānārthikebhyaḥ | [LalVis, 6 20.2]
evaṃ gandhamālyavilepanaśayyopāśrayaṃ prājīvikaṃ prājīvikārthibhyo yāvadeva bodhisattvasya pūjākarmaṇe | [LalVis, 6 20.3]
atha khalu bhikṣavo rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyaitadabhavat katamasmin gṛhe māyādevī sukham anupakliṣṭā viharediti | [LalVis, 6 21.1]
atha tatkṣaṇameva catvāro mahārājāno rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramyaivamāhuḥ | [LalVis, 6 21.2]
alpotsuko deva bhava sukhaṃ tiṣṭha upekṣako | [LalVis, 6 22.1]
vayaṃ hi bodhisattvasya veśma vai māpayāmahe | [LalVis, 6 22.2]
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ sarvaiḥ kāmāvacarair deveśvarairbodhisattvasya pūjārthaṃ kapilāhvaye mahāpuravare svakasvakāni gṛhāṇi māpitānyabhūvan | [LalVis, 6 35.1]
rājñā cāpi śuddhodanena manuṣyātikrāntaṃ divyāsaṃprāptaṃ gṛhataraṃ pratisaṃskāritamabhūt | [LalVis, 6 35.2]
tatra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mahāvyūhasya samādheranubhāvena sarveṣu teṣu gṛheṣu māyādevīmupadarśayati sma | [LalVis, 6 35.3]
abhyantaragataśca bodhisattvo māyādevyāḥ kukṣau dakṣiṇe pārśve paryaṅkamābhujya niṣaṇṇo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 6 35.4]
sarve ca te deveśvarā ekaikamevaṃ saṃjānīte sma mamaiva gṛhe bodhisattvamātā prativasati nānyatreti | [LalVis, 6 35.5]
atha khalu tasyāṃ devaparṣadi keṣāṃciddevaputrāṇāmetadabhavad ye 'pi tāvaccāturmahārājakāyikā devāste 'pi tāvanmanuṣyāśrayagatatvena nirvidyāpakramanti | [LalVis, 6 38.1]
kaḥ punarvādo ye tadanye udāratamā devāḥ trāyatriṃśā vā yāmā vā tuṣitā vā | [LalVis, 6 38.2]
tatkathaṃ hi nāma sarvalokābhyudgato bodhisattvaḥ śucirnirāmagandhaḥ sattvaratnaḥ saṃtuṣitāddevanikāyāccyutvā durgandhe manuṣyāśraye daśamāsān mātuḥ kukṣau sthita iti | [LalVis, 6 38.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmānānando buddhānubhāvena bhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yāvajjugupsanīyaśca mātṛgrāmastathāgatenokto yāvadrāgacaritaśca | [LalVis, 6 39.1]
idaṃ tu bhagavan āścaryataram | [LalVis, 6 39.2]
kathaṃ hi nāma sarvalokābhyudgato bhagavān pūrvaṃ bodhisattvabhūta eva tuṣitāddevanikāyāccyavitvā manuṣyāśraye durgandhe māturdakṣiṇe pārśve kukṣāvupapanna iti | [LalVis, 6 39.3]
nāhaṃ bhagavan idamutsahe evaṃ vaktuṃ yathaiva pūrve bhagavatā vyākṛtamiti | [LalVis, 6 39.4]
bhagavānāha icchasi tvamānanda ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ draṣṭuṃ yo mātuḥ kukṣigatasya bodhisattvasya paribhogo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 6 39.5]
ānanda āha ayamasya bhagavan kālaḥ ayaṃ sugata samayaḥ yattathāgatastaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogamupadarśayed yaṃ dṛṣṭvā prītiṃ vetsyāmaḥ | [LalVis, 6 39.6]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstathārūpanimittamakarot yad brahmā sahāpatiḥ sārdhamaṣṭaṣaṣṭibrahmaśatasahasrair brahmaloke 'ntarhito bhagavataḥ purataḥ pratyasthāt | [LalVis, 6 40.1]
sa bhagavataḥ pādau śirasābhivandya bhagavantaṃ tripradakṣiṇīkṛtyaikānte 'sthāt prāñjalībhūto bhagavantaṃ namasyan | [LalVis, 6 40.2]
tatra khalu bhagavān jānanneva brahmāṇaṃ sahāpatimāmantrayate sma gṛhītastvayā brahman sa bodhisattvaparibhogo daśamāsiko yo mama pūrvaṃ bodhisattvabhūtasya mātuḥ kukṣigatasyābhūt | [LalVis, 6 40.3]
brahmā āha evametadbhagavan evametat sugata | [LalVis, 6 40.4]
bhagavānāha kva sa idānīṃ brahman upadarśaya tam | [LalVis, 6 40.5]
brahmā cāha brahmaloke sa bhagavan | [LalVis, 6 40.6]
bhagavānāha tena hi tvaṃ brahman upadarśaya taṃ daśamāsikaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ jñāsyanti kiyatsaṃskṛtamiti | [LalVis, 6 40.7]
atha khalu brahmā sahāpatistān brāhmaṇānetadavocat tiṣṭhatu tāvadbhavanto yāvadvayaṃ ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogamānayiṣyāmaḥ | [LalVis, 6 41.1]
atha khalu brahmā sahāpatirbhagavataḥ pādau śirasābhivanditvā bhagavataḥ purato 'ntarhitastatkṣaṇameva brahmaloke pratyasthāt | [LalVis, 6 42.1]
atha khalu brahmā sahāpatiḥ subrahmāṇaṃ devaputrametadavocat gaccha tvaṃ mārṣā ito brahmalokamupādāya yāvattrāyatriṃśadbhavanaṃ śabdamudīraya ghoṣamanuśrāvaya | [LalVis, 6 43.1]
ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ vayaṃ tathāgatasyāntikamupanāmayiṣyāmaḥ | [LalVis, 6 43.2]
yo yuṣmākaṃ draṣṭukāmaḥ sa śīghramāgacchatviti | [LalVis, 6 43.3]
atha khalu brahmā sahāpatiścaturaśītyā devakoṭyā nayutaśatasahasraḥ sārdhaṃ taṃ ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ parigṛhya mahati brāhme vimāne triyojanaśatike pratiṣṭhāpyānekair daivakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraiḥ samantato 'nuparivārya jambūdvīpamavatārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 44.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena kāmāvacarāṇāṃ devānāṃ mahāsaṃnipāto 'bhūt bhagavatsakāśe gantum | [LalVis, 6 45.1]
sa khalu punā ratnavyūho bodhisattvaparibhogo divyairvastrairdivyairmālyair divyairgandhairdivyaiḥ puṣpairdivyairvādyairdivyaiśca paribhogairabhisaṃskṛto 'bhūt | [LalVis, 6 45.2]
tāvanmaheśākhyaiśca devaiḥ parivṛto 'bhūd yacchakro devānāmindraḥ sumerau sthitvā dūrata eva mukhe tālacchatrakaṃ dattvā śīrṣavyavalokanenānuvilokayati sma unmeṣadhyāyikayā vā | [LalVis, 6 45.3]
na ca śaknoti sma draṣṭum | [LalVis, 6 45.4]
tatkasmāt maheśākhyā hi devā brāhmaṇāḥ | [LalVis, 6 45.5]
itarāstrāyatriṃśā yāmāstuṣitā nirmāṇaratayaḥ paranirmitavaśavartinaḥ | [LalVis, 6 45.6]
kaḥ punarvādaḥ śakro devānāmindraḥ | [LalVis, 6 45.7]
mohaṃ te vai yānti sma | [LalVis, 6 45.8]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstaṃ divyaṃ vādyanirghoṣamantardhāpayati sma | [LalVis, 6 46.1]
tatkasmāt yatsahaśravaṇādeva jāmbudvīpakā manuṣyā unmādamāpatsyanta iti | [LalVis, 6 46.2]
atha khalu catvāro mahārājānaḥ śakraṃ devānāmindramupasaṃkramyaivamāhuḥ kathaṃ devānāmindra kariṣyāmo na labhāmahe ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ draṣṭum | [LalVis, 6 47.1]
sa tānavocat kimahaṃ mārṣāḥ kariṣyāmi ahamapi na labhe draṣṭum | [LalVis, 6 47.2]
api tu khalu punarmārṣā bhagavatsamīpamupanītaṃ drakṣyāmaḥ | [LalVis, 6 47.3]
te tadā āhus tena hi devānāmindra tathā kuru yathāsya kṣipraṃ darśanaṃ bhavet | [LalVis, 6 47.4]
śakra āha āgamayata mārṣā muhūrtaṃ yāvadatikrāntātikrāntatamā devaputrā bhagavantaṃ pratisaṃmodayante sma | [LalVis, 6 47.5]
tadekānte sthitvā śīrṣonmiñjitakayā bhagavantamanuvilokayanti sma | [LalVis, 6 47.6]
atha khalu brahmā sahāpatiḥ sārdhaṃ taiścaturaśītyā devakoṭīnayutaśatasahasraistaṃ ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ gṛhītvā yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāmayati sma | [LalVis, 6 48.1]
sa khalu puna ratnavyūho bodhisattvaparibhogo 'bhirūpaḥ prāsādiko darśanīyaścaturasraścatuṣṭhūṇaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.2]
upariṣṭācca kūṭāgārasamalaṃkṛtaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.3]
evaṃpramāṇaḥ tadyathāpi nāma ṣaṇmāsajāto dāraka uccaistvena | [LalVis, 6 48.4]
tasya khalu punaḥ kūṭāgārasya madhye paryaṅkaḥ prajñaptaḥ tadyathāpi nāma ṣaṇmāsajātasya dārakasya bhittīphalakaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.5]
sa khalu puna ratnavyūho bodhisattvaparibhoga evaṃ varṇasaṃsthāno yasya na kaścit sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sadṛśo 'sti ākṛtyā vā varṇena vā | [LalVis, 6 48.6]
devāḥ khalvapi taṃ dṛṣṭvā āścaryaprāptā abhuvan | [LalVis, 6 48.7]
cakṣūṃṣi teṣāṃ vibhramanti sma | [LalVis, 6 48.8]
sa ca tathāgatasyāntika upanīto 'tīva bhāsate tapati virocate sma | [LalVis, 6 48.9]
tadyathāpi nāma dvinirdhāntaṃ suvarṇaṃ kuśalena karmakāreṇa supariniṣṭhitamapagatakācadoṣam evaṃ tasmin samaye sa kūṭāgāro virājate sma | [LalVis, 6 48.10]
tasmin khalu punarbodhisattvaparibhoge paryaṅkaḥ prajñapto yasya sadevake loke nāsti kaścit sadṛśo varṇena vā saṃsthānena vā anyatra kambugrīvāyā bodhisattvasya | [LalVis, 6 48.11]
yat khalu mahābrahmaṇā cīvaraṃ prāvṛtamabhūt tattasya bodhisattvaparyaṅkasyāgrato na bhāsate sma tadyathāpi nāma vātavṛṣṭyābhihataḥ kṛṣṇakambalaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.12]
sa khalu punaḥ kūṭāgāra uragasāracandanamayo yasyaikasuvarṇadharaṇī sāhasraṃ lokadhātuṃ mūlyaṃ kṣamate tathāvidhenoragasāracandanena sa kūṭāgāraḥ samantād anupaliptaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.13]
tādṛśa eva dvitīyaḥ kūṭāgāraḥ kṛto yastasmin prathame kūṭāgāre 'bhyantarataḥ asakto 'baddhasthitaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.14]
tādṛśa eva tṛtīyo 'pi kūṭāgāro yastasmin dvitīye kūṭāgāre 'bhyantare 'sakto 'baddhasthitaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.15]
sa ca paryaṅkastasmin gandhamaye tṛtīye kūṭāgāre vyavasthitaḥ saṃpraticchannaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.16]
tasya khalu punaruragasāracandanasyaivaṃrūpo varṇaḥ tadyathāpi nāma abhijātasya nīlavaiḍūryasya | [LalVis, 6 48.17]
tasya khalu punargandhakūṭāgārasyopari samantādyāvanti kāniciddivyātikrāntāni puṣpāṇi santi tāni sarvāṇi tasmin kūṭāgāre bodhisattvasya pūrvakuśalamūlavipākenānuprāptānyeva jāyante sma | [LalVis, 6 48.18]
sa khalu puna ratnavyūho bodhisattvaparibhogo dṛḍhasāro 'bhedyo vajropamaḥ sparśena ca kācilindikasukhasaṃsparśaḥ | [LalVis, 6 48.19]
tasmin khalu puna ratnavyūhe bodhisattvaparibhoge ye kecit kāmāvacarāṇāṃ devānāṃ bhavanavyūhāste sarve tasmin saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 6 48.20]
yāmeva ca rātriṃ bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣimavakrāntastāmeva rātrimadha āpaskandhamupādāya aṣṭaṣaṣṭiyojanaśatasahasrāṇi mahāpṛthivīṃ bhittvā yāvad brahmalokaṃ padmamabhyudgatamabhūt | [LalVis, 6 49.1]
na ca kaścittaṃ padmaṃ paśyati sma anyatra sārathinarottamād daśaśatasāhasrikācca mahābrahmaṇaḥ | [LalVis, 6 49.2]
yacceha trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātāvojo vā maṇḍo vā raso vā tatsarvaṃ tasmin mahāpadme madhubinduḥ saṃtiṣṭhate sma | [LalVis, 6 49.3]
tamenaṃ mahābrahmā śubhe vaiḍūryabhājane prakṣipya bodhisattvasyopanāmayati sma | [LalVis, 6 50.1]
taṃ bodhisattvaḥ parigṛhya bhuṅkte sma mahābrahmaṇo 'nukampāmupādāya | [LalVis, 6 50.2]
nāsti sa kaścit sattvaḥ sattvanikāye yasya sa ojobinduḥ paribhuktaḥ samyak sukhena pariṇamedanyatra caramabhavikādbodhisattvāt sarvabodhisattvabhūmiparipūrṇāt | [LalVis, 6 50.3]
kasya ca karmaṇo vipākena sa ojobindurbodhisattvasyopatiṣṭhate sma dīrgharātraṃ khalvapi bodhisattvena pūrvaṃ bodhisattvacaryāṃ caratā glānebhyaḥ sattvebhyo bhaiṣajyaṃ dattam āśatparāṇāṃ sattvānāmāśāḥ paripūritāḥ śaraṇāgatāśca na parityaktāḥ nityaṃ cāgrapuṣpamagraphalamagrarasaṃ tathāgatebhyastathāgatacaityebhyas tathāgataśrāvakasaṃghebhyo mātāpitṛbhyaśca dattvā paścādātmanā paribhuktam | [LalVis, 6 50.4]
tasya karmaṇo vipākena mahābrahmā bodhisattvasya taṃ madhubindumupanāmayati sma | [LalVis, 6 50.5]
tasmin khalu punaḥ kūṭāgāre yāni kānicit santyatikrāntātikrāntāni māyāguṇaratikrīḍāsamavasṛtasthānāni tāni sarvāṇi tasmin prādurbhāvāni saṃdṛśyante sma bodhisattvasya pūrvakarmavipākena | [LalVis, 6 51.1]
tasmin khalu puna ratnavyūhe bodhisattvaparibhoge śatasahasravyūhaṃ nāma vāsoyugaṃ prādurbhūtam | [LalVis, 6 52.1]
na sa kaścitsattvaḥ sattvanikāye saṃvidyate yasya tatprādurbhavedanyatra caramabhavikād bodhisattvāt | [LalVis, 6 52.2]
na ca te kecana udārodārā rūpaśabdagandharasasparśā ye tasmin kūṭāgāre na saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 6 52.3]
sacetkūṭāgāraparibhoga evaṃ suparibhoga evaṃ supariniṣpannaḥ sāntarabahirevaṃ supariniṣṭhita evaṃ mṛdukaśca | [LalVis, 6 52.4]
tadyathāpi nāma kācilindikasukhasaṃsparśo nidarśanamātreṇa na tu tasyopamā saṃvidyate | [LalVis, 6 52.5]
dharmatā khalveṣā bodhisattvasya pūrvakeṇa ca praṇidhānena iyaṃ cetanā ṛddhāvavaśyaṃ bodhisattvena mahāsattvena manuṣyaloka upapattavyamabhiniṣkramya cānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya dharmacakraṃ pravartayitavyam | [LalVis, 6 52.6]
yasyā mātuḥ kukṣāvupapattirbhavati tasyā dakṣiṇe kukṣāvādita eva ratnavyūhakūṭāgāro 'bhinirvartate | [LalVis, 6 52.7]
paścādbodhisattvastuṣitebhyaścyuttvā tasmin kūṭāgāre paryaṅkaniṣaṇṇaḥ sambhavati | [LalVis, 6 52.8]
na hi caramabhavikasya bodhisattvasya kalalārbudaghanapeśībhāvaṃ kāyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate sma | [LalVis, 6 52.9]
atha tarhi sarvāṅgapratyaṅgalakṣaṇasampannaḥ saṃniṣaṇṇa eva prādurbhavati | [LalVis, 6 52.10]
svapnāntaragatā ca bodhisattvamātā māyādevī mahānāgakuñjaramavakrāntaṃ saṃjānīte sma | [LalVis, 6 52.11]
tasya khalu punastathā niṣaṇṇasya śakro devānāmindraścatvāraśca mahārājāno 'ṣṭāviṃśatiśca mahāyakṣasenāpatayo guhyakādhipatiśca nāma yakṣakulaṃ yato vajrapāṇerutpattiste bodhisattvaṃ mātuḥ kukṣigataṃ viditvā satataṃ samitamanubaddhā bhavanti sma | [LalVis, 6 53.1]
santi khalu punaścatasro bodhisattvaparicārakā devatāḥ utkhalī ca nāma samutkhalī ca nāma dhvajavatī ca nāma prabhāvatī ca nāma | [LalVis, 6 53.2]
tā api bodhisattvaṃ mātuḥ kukṣigataṃ viditvā satataṃ samitaṃ rakṣanti sma | [LalVis, 6 53.3]
śakro 'pi devānāmindraḥ sārdhaṃ pañcamātrairdevaputraśatairbodhisattvaṃ mātuḥ kukṣigataṃ jñātvā satataṃ samitamanubadhnāti sma | [LalVis, 6 53.4]
bodhisattvasya khalu punarmātuḥ kukṣigatasya kāyastathāvidho 'bhūt tadyathāpi nāma parvatamūrdhani rātrāvandhakāratamisrāyāṃ mahānagniskandho yojanādapi dṛśyate sma yāvat pañcabhyo yojanebhyo dṛśyate sma | [LalVis, 6 54.1]
evameva bodhisattvasya mātuḥ kukṣigatasyātmabhāvo 'bhinirvṛtto 'bhūt prabhāsvaro 'bhirūpaḥ prāsādiko darśanīyaḥ | [LalVis, 6 54.2]
sa tasmin kūṭāgāre paryaṅkaniṣaṇṇo 'tīva śobhate sma | [LalVis, 6 54.3]
vaiḍūryapratyuptamivābhijātaṃ jātarūpam | [LalVis, 6 54.4]
bodhisattvasya mātā ca nidhyāya sthitā paśyati sma kukṣigataṃ bodhisattvam | [LalVis, 6 54.5]
tadyathāpi nāma mahato 'bhrakūṭādvidyuto niḥsṛtya mahāntamavabhāsaṃ saṃjanayanti evameva bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣigataḥ śriyā tejasā varṇena ca taṃ prathamaṃ ratnakūṭāgāramavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.6]
avabhāsya dvitīyaṃ gandhakūṭāgāramavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.7]
dvitīyaṃ gandhakūṭāgāramavabhāsya tṛtīyaṃ ratnakūṭāgāramavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.8]
tṛtīyaṃ ratnakūṭāgāramavabhāsya sarvāvantaṃ māturātmabhāvamavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.9]
tamavabhāsya yatra cāsane niṣaṇṇo bhavati sma tadavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.10]
tadavabhāsya sarvaṃ gṛhamavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.11]
sarvaṃ gṛhamavabhāsya gṛhasyopariṣṭānniḥsṛtya pūrvāṃ diśamavabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.12]
evaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ paścimāṃ uttarāmadha ūrdhvaṃ samantāddaśadiśaḥ krośamātramekaikasyāṃ diśi mātuḥ kukṣigato bodhisattvaḥ śriyā tejasā varṇena cāvabhāsayati sma | [LalVis, 6 54.13]
āgacchanti sma khalu punarbhikṣavaścatvāro mahārājāno 'ṣṭāviṃśacca mahāyakṣasenāpatayaḥ sārdhaṃ pañcamātrayakṣaśataiḥ pūrvāhṇakālasamaye bodhisattvasya darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya dharmaśravaṇāya ca | [LalVis, 6 55.1]
tadā bodhisattvastānāgatān viditvā dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim abhyutkṣipya ekāṅgulikayā āsanānyupadarśayati sma | [LalVis, 6 55.2]
niṣīdanti sma te lokapālādayo yathāprajñapteṣvāsaneṣu | [LalVis, 6 55.3]
paśyanti sma bodhisattvaṃ mātuḥ kukṣigataṃ jātarūpamiva vigrahaṃ hastaṃ cālayantaṃ vicālayantam utkṣipantaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayantam | [LalVis, 6 55.4]
te prītiprāmodyaprasādapratilabdhā bodhisattvaṃ namaskurvanti sma | [LalVis, 6 55.5]
niṣaṇṇāṃśca tān viditvā bodhisattvo dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati sma samādāpayati sma samuttejayati sma saṃpraharṣayati sma | [LalVis, 6 55.6]
yadā ca prakramitukāmā bhavanti tadā bodhisattvasteṣāṃ cetasaiva vicintitaṃ vijñāya dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇimutkṣipya saṃcārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 55.7]
saṃcārya vicārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 55.8]
mātaraṃ ca na bādhate sma | [LalVis, 6 55.9]
tadā teṣāṃ caturṇāṃ mahārājānāmevaṃ bhavati sma visarjitāḥ sma vayaṃ bodhisattveneti | [LalVis, 6 55.10]
te bodhisattvaṃ bodhisattvamātaraṃ ca tripradakṣiṇīkṛtya prakrāmanti sma | [LalVis, 6 55.11]
ayaṃ heturayaṃ pratyayo yadbodhisattvo rātryāṃ praśāntāyāṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇiṃ saṃcārya vicārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 55.12]
vicārya punarapi smṛtaḥ samprajānaṃstaṃ pāṇiṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati sma | [LalVis, 6 55.13]
punaraparaṃ yadā bodhisattvasya keciddarśanāyāgacchanti sma striyo vā puruṣo vā dārako vā dārikā vā tān bodhisattvaḥ pūrvatarameva pratisaṃmodayate sma paścādbodhisattvasya mātā | [LalVis, 6 55.14]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣigataḥ san sattvān pratisaṃmodanakuśalo bhavati smeti | [LalVis, 6 56.1]
na ca kaściddevo vā nāgo vā yakṣo vā manuṣyo vā amanuṣyo vā yaḥ śaknoti sma bodhisattvaṃ pūrvataraṃ pratisaṃmoditum | [LalVis, 6 56.2]
atha tarhi bodhisattva eva tāvat pūrvataraṃ pratisaṃmodate sma paścādbodhisattvamātā | [LalVis, 6 56.3]
nirgate khalu punaḥ pūrvāhṇakālasamaye madhyāhnakālasamaye pratyupasthite atha khalu śakro devānāmindro niṣkrāntaḥ | [LalVis, 6 57.1]
abhiniṣkrāntāśca trāyatriṃśaddevaputrā bodhisattvasya darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya | [LalVis, 6 57.2]
dharmaśravaṇāya cāgacchanti sma | [LalVis, 6 57.3]
tāṃśca bodhisattvo dūrata evāgacchato dṛṣṭvā dakṣiṇaṃ suvarṇavarṇaṃ bāhuṃ prasārya śakraṃ devānāmindraṃ devāṃśca trāyatriṃśān pratisaṃmodate sma | [LalVis, 6 57.4]
ekāṅgulikayā cāsanānyupadarśayati sma | [LalVis, 6 57.5]
na ca śaknoti sma bhikṣavaḥ śakro devānāmindro bodhisattvasyājñāṃ pratiroddhum | [LalVis, 6 57.6]
niṣīdati sma śakro devānāmindrastadanye ca devaputrā yathāprajñapteṣvāsaneṣu | [LalVis, 6 57.7]
tān bodhisattvo niṣaṇṇān viditvā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati sma samādāpayati sma samuttejayati sma saṃpraharṣayati sma | [LalVis, 6 57.8]
yena ca bodhisattvaḥ pāṇiṃ saṃcārayati sma tanmukhā bodhisattvamātā bhavati sma | [LalVis, 6 57.9]
tatasteṣāmevaṃ bhavati sma asmābhiḥ sārdhaṃ bodhisattvaḥ saṃmodate sma | [LalVis, 6 57.10]
ekaikaścaivaṃ saṃjānīte sma mayaiva sārdhaṃ bodhisattvaḥ saṃlapati māmeva pratisaṃmodate sma iti | [LalVis, 6 57.11]
tasmin khalu punaḥ kūṭāgāre śakrasya devānāmindrasya trāyatriṃśānāṃ devānāṃ ca pratibhāsaḥ saṃdṛśyate sma | [LalVis, 6 58.1]
na khalu punaranyatraivaṃ pariśuddho bodhisattvaparibhogo bhavati yathā mātuḥ kukṣigatasya bodhisattvasya | [LalVis, 6 58.2]
yadā ca bhikṣavaḥ śakro devānāmindrastadanye ca devaputrāḥ prakramitukāmā bhavanti sma tadā bodhisattvasteṣāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇimutkṣipya saṃcārayanti sma | [LalVis, 6 58.3]
saṃcārya vicārya punarapi smṛtaḥ samprajānan pratiṣṭhāpayati sma | [LalVis, 6 58.4]
mātaraṃ ca na bādhate sma | [LalVis, 6 58.5]
tadā śakrasya devānāmindrasyānyeṣāṃ ca trāyatriṃśānāṃ devānāmevaṃ bhavati sma visarjitā vayaṃ bodhisattveneti | [LalVis, 6 58.6]
te bodhisattvaṃ bodhisattvamātaraṃ ca tripradakṣiṇīkṛtya prakrāmanti sma | [LalVis, 6 58.7]
nirgate ca khalu punarbhikṣavo madhyāhnakālasamaye sāyāhnakālasamaye pratyupasthite atha khalu brahmā sahāpatiranekairbrahmakāyikair devaputraśatasahasraiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛtastaṃ divyamojobindumādāya yena bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāmati sma bodhisattvaṃ draṣṭuṃ vandituṃ paryupāsituṃ dharmaṃ ca śrotum | [LalVis, 6 59.1]
samanvāharati sma bhikṣavaḥ bodhisattvo brahmāṇaṃ sahāpatimāgacchantaṃ saparivāram | [LalVis, 6 59.2]
punareva ca bodhisattvo dakṣiṇaṃ suvarṇavarṇapāṇimutkṣipya brahmāṇaṃ sahāpatiṃ brahmakāyikāṃśca devaputrān pratisaṃmodate sma | [LalVis, 6 59.3]
ekāṅgulikayā cāsanānyupadarśayati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.4]
na ca śaktirasti bhikṣavo brahmaṇaḥ sahāpaterbodhisattvasyājñāṃ pratiroddhum | [LalVis, 6 59.5]
niṣīdati sma bhikṣavo brahmā sahāpatistadanye ca brahmakāyikā devaputrā yathāprajñapteṣvāsaneṣu | [LalVis, 6 59.6]
tān bodhisattvo niṣaṇṇān viditvā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati sma samādāpayati sma samuttejayati sma saṃpraharṣayati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.7]
yena ca bodhisattvaḥ pāṇiṃ saṃcārayati sma tanmukhaiva māyādevī bhavati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.8]
tatasteṣāmekaikasyaivaṃ bhavati sma mayā sārdhaṃ bodhisattvaḥ saṃlapati māmeva pratisaṃmodate sma iti | [LalVis, 6 59.9]
yadā ca brahmā sahāpatistadanye ca brahmakāyikā devaputrā gantukāmā bhavanti sma tadā bodhisattvasteṣāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya dakṣiṇaṃ suvarṇavarṇaṃ bāhumutkṣipya saṃcārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.10]
saṃcārya vicārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.11]
saṃcārya vicārya avasādatākāreṇa pāṇiṃ saṃcārayati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.12]
mātaraṃ ca na bādhate sma | [LalVis, 6 59.13]
tato brahmaṇaḥ sahāpatestadanyeṣāṃ ca brahmakāyikānāṃ devaputrāṇāmevaṃ bhavati sma visarjitā vayaṃ bodhisattveneti | [LalVis, 6 59.14]
te bodhisattvaṃ bodhisattvamātaraṃ ca tripradakṣiṇīkṛtya punareva prakrāmanti sma | [LalVis, 6 59.15]
bodhisattvaśca smṛtaḥ samprajānan pāṇiṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati sma | [LalVis, 6 59.16]
āgacchanti sma khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ pūrvadakṣiṇapaścimottarābhyo digbhyo 'dhastādupariṣṭāt santāddaśabhyo digbhyo bahūni bodhisattvaśatasahasrāṇi bodhisattvasya darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya dharmaśravaṇāya ca dharmasaṃgītisaṃgāyanāya ca | [LalVis, 6 60.1]
teṣāmāgatāgatānāṃ bodhisattvaḥ kāyāt prabhāmutsṛjya prabhāvyūhāni siṃhāsanānyabhinirmimīte sma | [LalVis, 6 60.2]
abhinirmāya tān bodhisattvāṃsteṣvāsaneṣu niṣīdayati sma | [LalVis, 6 60.3]
niṣaṇṇāṃścainān viditvā paripṛcchati sma paripraśnayati sma yadutāsyaiva bodhisattvasya mahāyānasya vistaravibhāgatāmupādāya | [LalVis, 6 60.4]
na ca tān kaścidanyaḥ paśyati sma anyatra sabhāgebhyo devaputrebhyaḥ | [LalVis, 6 60.5]
ayaṃ bhikṣavo heturayaṃ pratyayo yena bodhisattvaḥ praśāntāyāṃ rātryāṃ kāyāt prabhāmutsṛjati sma | [LalVis, 6 60.6]
na khalu punarbhikṣavo māyādevī bodhisattvakukṣigate gurukāyatāṃ saṃjānīte sma anyatra laghutāmeva mṛdutāmeva saukhyatāmeva | [LalVis, 6 61.1]
na codaragatāni duḥkhāni pratyanubhavati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.2]
na ca rāgaparidāhena vā dveṣaparidāhena vā mohaparidāhena vā paridahyate sma | [LalVis, 6 61.3]
na ca kāmavitarkaṃ vā vyāpādavitarkaṃ vā vihiṃsāvitarkaṃ vā vitarkayati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.4]
na ca śītaṃ na coṣṇaṃ vā jighatsāṃ vā pipāsāṃ vā tamo vā rajo vā kleśaṃ vā saṃjānīte sma paśyati vā | [LalVis, 6 61.5]
na cāsyā amanāpā rūpaśabdagandharasasparśā vā ābhāsamāgacchanti sma | [LalVis, 6 61.6]
na ca pāpakān svapnān paśyati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.7]
na cāsyāḥ strīmāyā na śāṭhyaṃ nerṣyā na strīkleśā bādhante sma | [LalVis, 6 61.8]
pañcaśikṣāpadasamādattā khalu punaḥ śīlavatī daśakuśalakarmapathe pratiṣṭhitā tasmin samaye bodhisattvamātā bhavati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.9]
na ca bodhisattvamātuḥ kvacit puruṣe rāgacittamutpadyate sma nāpi kasyacitpuruṣasya bodhisattvasya māturantike | [LalVis, 6 61.10]
ye ca kecitkapilāhvaye mahāpuravare anyeṣu vā janapadeṣu devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍabhūtāviṣṭāḥ strīpuruṣadārakadārikā vā te sarve bodhisattvamātuḥ sahadarśanādeva svasthāḥ smṛtipratilabdhā bhavanti sma | [LalVis, 6 61.11]
te cāmanuṣyāḥ kṣiprameva prakrāmanti sma | [LalVis, 6 61.12]
ye ca kecinnānārogaspṛṣṭāḥ sattvā bhavanti sma vātapittaśleṣmasaṃnipātajai rogaiḥ pīḍyante sma cakṣurogeṇa vā śrotrarogeṇa vā ghrāṇarogeṇa vā jihvārogeṇa vā oṣṭharogeṇa vā dantarogeṇa kaṇṭharogeṇa vā galagaṇḍarogeṇa vā uragaṇḍakuṣṭhakilāsaśoṣonmādāpasmārajvaragalagaṇḍapiṭakavisarpavicarcikādyai rogaiḥ sampīḍyante sma teṣāṃ bodhisattvamātā dakṣiṇapāṇiṃ mūrdhni pratiṣṭhāpayati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.13]
te sahapratiṣṭhāpite pāṇau vigatavyādhayo bhūtvā svakasvakāni gṛhāṇi gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 6 61.14]
antato māyādevī tṛṇagulmakamapi dharaṇitalādabhyutkṣipya glānebhyaḥ sattvebhyo 'nuprayacchati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.15]
te sahapratilambhādaroganirvikārā bhavanti sma | [LalVis, 6 61.16]
yadā ca māyādevī svaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvaṃ pratyavekṣate sma tadā paśyati sma bodhisattvaṃ kukṣigataṃ tadyathāpi nāma supariśuddha ādarśamaṇḍale mukhamaṇḍalaṃ dṛśyate | [LalVis, 6 61.17]
dṛṣṭvā ca punastuṣṭā udagrā āttamanāḥ pramuditā prītisaumanasyajātā bhavati sma | [LalVis, 6 61.18]
bodhisattvasya khalu punarbhikṣavo mātuḥ kukṣigatasyādhiṣṭhitaṃ satataṃ samitaṃ rātriṃdivaṃ divyāni tūryāṇi abhinirmāya pranadanti sma | [LalVis, 6 62.1]
divyāni ca puṣpāṇi abhipravarṣanti sma | [LalVis, 6 62.2]
kālena devā varṣanti sma | [LalVis, 6 62.3]
kālena vāyavo vānti sma | [LalVis, 6 62.4]
kālena ṛtavo nakṣatrāṇi ca parivartante sma | [LalVis, 6 62.5]
kṣemaṃ ca rājyaṃ subhikṣaṃ ca sumanākulam anubhavati sma | [LalVis, 6 62.6]
sarve ca kapilāhvaye mahāpuravare śākyā anye ca sattvāḥ khādanti sma pibanti sma krīḍanti sma pravicārayanti sma dānāni ca dadanti sma puṇyāni ca kurvanti sma kaumodyāmiva cāturmāsyāmekāntare krīḍāsukhavihārairviharanti sma | [LalVis, 6 62.7]
rājāpi śuddhodanaḥ samprāptabrahmacaryoparatarāṣṭrakāryo 'pi supariśuddhastapovanagata iva dharmamevānuvartate sma | [LalVis, 6 62.8]
evaṃrūpeṇa bhikṣava ṛddhiprātihāryeṇa samanvāgato bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣigato 'sthāt | [LalVis, 6 63.1]
tatra khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate sma drakṣyasi tvamānanda ratnavyūhaṃ bodhisattvaparibhogaṃ yatra bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣigato vyāhārṣīt | [LalVis, 6 63.2]
āha paśyeyaṃ bhagavan paśyeyaṃ sugata | [LalVis, 6 63.3]
darśayati sma tathāgata āyuṣmata ānandasya śakrasya devānāmindrasya caturṇāṃ ca lokapālānāṃ tadanyeṣāṃ ca devamanuṣyāṇām | [LalVis, 6 63.4]
dṛṣṭvā ca te tuṣṭā abhūvan udagrā āttamanasaḥ pramuditāḥ prītisaumanasyajātāḥ | [LalVis, 6 63.5]
sa ca brahmā sahāpatiḥ punareva brahmaloke samāropya pratiṣṭhāpayati sma caityārtham | [LalVis, 6 63.6]
tatra khalu bhagavān punarapi bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma iti hi bhikṣavo daśamāsakukṣigatena bodhisattvena ṣaṭtriṃśannayutāni devamanuṣyāṇāṃ triṣu yāneṣu paripācitānyabhūvan | [LalVis, 6 64.1]
yatredamucyate yat | [LalVis, 6 64.2]
{LalVis, 7}
iti hi bhikṣavo daśamāseṣu nigateṣu bodhisattvasya janmakālasamaye pratyupasthite rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhodyāne dvātriṃśatpūrvanimittāni prādurabhūvan | [LalVis, 7 1.1]
katamāni dvātriṃśat sarvapuṣpāṇi suṅgībhūtāni na puṣpanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.2]
puṣkariṇīṣu cotpalapadmakumudapuṇḍarīkāṇyabhyudgatāni kuḍmalībhūtāni na puṣpanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.3]
tadā ca puṣpaphalavṛkṣā dharaṇītalādabhyudgamya kṣārakajātā na phalanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.4]
aṣṭau ca ratnavṛkṣāḥ prādurabhūvan | [LalVis, 7 1.5]
viṃśati ca ratnanidhānaśatasahasrāṇyutplutya vyavasthitāni dṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.6]
antaḥpure ca ratnāṅkurāḥ prādurabhūvan | [LalVis, 7 1.7]
sugandhitailaparivāsitāśca gandhodakaśītoṣṇāḥ prasravanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.8]
himavatparvatapārśvācca siṃhapotakā āgatyāgatyābhinadantaḥ kapilāhvayapuravaraṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dvāramūleṣvavatiṣṭhante sma na kaṃcitsattvaṃ viheṭhayanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.9]
pañcaśatāni pāṇḍarāṇāṃ hastiśāvakānāmāgatya rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyāgrakaraiścaraṇāvabhilikhanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.10]
mekhalībaddhakāśca devadārakā rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyāntaḥpure utsaṅgenotsaṅgamanuparivartamānāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.11]
gaganatalagatārdhakāyā nāgakanyā nānāpūjopakaraṇaparigṛhītā adhyālambamānāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.12]
daśa ca nāgakanyāsahasrāṇi mayūrāṅgahastakaparigṛhītā gaganatale 'vasthitāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.13]
daśa ca pūrṇakumbhasahasrāṇi kapilavastu mahānagaraṃ pradakṣiṇīkurvanti saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.14]
daśa ca devakanyāsahasrāṇi gandhodakabhṛṅgāraparigṛhītā mūrdhni dhārayantyo 'vasthitāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.15]
daśa ca devakanyāsahasrāṇi chatradhvajapatākāparigṛhītā avasthitāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.16]
bahūni cāpsaraḥśatasahasrāṇi śaṅkhabherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavaiḥ ghaṇṭāvasaktaiḥ pratīkṣamāṇānyavasthitāni saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.17]
sarve vāyavaścāvasthitā na vānti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.18]
sarvanadī ca prasravaṇāni ca na vahanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.19]
candrasūryavimānāni nakṣatrajyotirgaṇāśca na vahanti sma | [LalVis, 7 1.20]
puṣyaṃ ca nakṣatrayuktamabhūt | [LalVis, 7 1.21]
ratnajālaparisphuṭaṃ ca rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhaṃ saṃsthitamabhūt | [LalVis, 7 1.22]
vaiśvānaraśca na jvalati sma | [LalVis, 7 1.23]
kūṭāgāraprāsādatoraṇadvārakataleṣu ca maṇiratnānyabhipralambamānāni ca saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.24]
dūṣyagañjāśca viviratnagañjāśca prāvṛtāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.25]
kākolūkagṛdhravṛkaśṛgālaśabdāścāntarhitā abhūvan | [LalVis, 7 1.26]
sujātajātaśabdāśca śrūyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.27]
sarvajanapadakarmāntāśca samucchinnā abhūvan | [LalVis, 7 1.28]
utkūlanikūlāśca pṛthivīpradeśāḥ samāḥ samavasthitāḥ sarvavīthīcatvaraśṛṅgāṭakarathyāntarāpaṇamukhāni ca pāṇitalamṛṣṭānīva puṣpābhikīrṇāni virocante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.29]
sarvāśca gurviṇyaḥ samyaksukhena prasūyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.30]
sarvaśālavanadevatāśca patreṣvardhakāyānabhinirmāya namyamānāḥ sthitāḥ saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 7 1.31]
imāni dvātriṃśatpūrvanimittāni prādurabhūvan | [LalVis, 7 1.32]
atha khalu māyādevī bodhisattvasya janmakālasamayaṃ jñātvā bodhisattvasyaiva tejo'nubhāvena rātryāṃ prathame yāme rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramya gāthābhirabhyabhāṣata | [LalVis, 7 2.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavo māyādevī caturaśītyā hayarathasahasraiḥ sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitaiḥ parivṛtā caturaśītyā gajarathasahasraiḥ sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitaiḥ caturaśītyā ca pattisahasraiḥ śūrairvīrairvarāṅgarūpibhiḥ susaṃnaddhadṛḍhavarmakavacitairanuparigṛhītā ṣaṣṭyā ca śākyakanyāsahasraiḥ puraskṛtā catvāriṃśatā ca sahasrai rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya jñātikulaprasūtaiḥ śākyaiḥ vṛddhadaharamadhyamaiḥ saṃrakṣitā ṣaṣṭyā ca sahasrai rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyāntaḥpureṇa gītavādyasamyaktūryatāḍāvacarasaṃgītisaṃpravāditena parivṛtā caturaśītyā ca devakanyāsahasraiḥ parivṛtā caturaśītyā ca nāgakanyāsahasraiḥ caturaśītyā ca gandharvakanyāsahasraiḥ caturaśītyā ca kinnarakanyāsahasraiḥ caturaśītyā cāsurakanyāsahasraiḥ nānāvyūhālaṃkārālaṃkṛtābhiḥ nānāgītavādyavarṇabhāṣiṇībhir anugamyamānā niryāti sma | [LalVis, 7 25.1]
sarvaṃ ca lumbinīvanaṃ gandhodakasiktaṃ divyapuṣpābhikīrṇīkṛtamabhūt | [LalVis, 7 25.2]
sarvavṛkṣāśca tasmin vanavare akālapatrapuṣpaphalāni dadanti sma | [LalVis, 7 25.3]
devaiśca tathā tadvanaṃ samalaṃkṛtamabhūt tadyathāpi nāma miśrakāvanaṃ devānāṃ samalaṃkṛtam | [LalVis, 7 25.4]
atha khalu māyādevī lumbinīvanamanupraviśya tasmādrathavarādavatīrya naramarukanyāparivṛtā vṛkṣeṇa vṛkṣaṃ paryaṭantī vanādvanaṃ caṅkramyamāṇā drumād drumaṃ nirīkṣamāṇā anupūrveṇa yenāsau plakṣo mahādrumaratnavarapravaraḥ suvibhaktaśākhaḥ samapatramañjarīdharo divyamānuṣyanānāpuṣpasaṃpuṣpito varapravarasurabhigandhinānāgandhinānāraṅgavastrābhipralambito vividhamaṇivicitraprabhojjvalitaḥ sarvaratnamūladaṇḍaśākhāpatrasamalaṃkṛtaḥ suvibhaktavistīrṇaśākhaḥ karatalanibhe bhūmibhāge suvibhaktavistīrṇanīlatṛṇamayūragrīvāsaṃnibhe kācilindikasukhasaṃsparśe dharaṇītale saṃsthitaḥ pūrvajinajanetryābhinivāsitaḥ devasaṃgītyanugītaḥ śubhavimalaviśuddhaḥ śuddhāvāsadevaśatasahasraiḥ praśāntacittair abhinatajaṭāmakuṭāvalambitāvanatamūrdhabhir abhinandyamānastaṃ plakṣavṛkṣamupajagāma | [LalVis, 7 26.1]
atha sa plakṣavṛkṣo bodhisattvasya tejo'nubhāvenāvanamya praṇamati sma | [LalVis, 7 27.1]
atha māyādevī gaganatalagateva vidyut dṛṣṭiṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ prasārya plakṣaśākhāṃ gṛhītvā salīlaṃ gaganatalaṃ prekṣamāṇā vijṛmbhamānā sthitābhūt | [LalVis, 7 27.2]
atha tasmin samaye ṣaṣṭyapsaraḥśatasahasrāṇi kāmāvacaradevebhya upasaṃkramya māyādevyā upasthāne paricaryāṃ kurvanti sma | [LalVis, 7 27.3]
evaṃrūpeṇa khalu puna ṛddhiprātihāryeṇa samanvāgato bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣigato 'sthāt | [LalVis, 7 28.1]
sa paripūrṇānāṃ daśānāṃ māsānāmatyayena māturdakṣiṇapārśvānniṣkramati sma smṛtaḥ samprajānannanupalipto garbhamalairyathā nānyaḥ kaściducyate 'nyeṣāṃ garbhamala iti | [LalVis, 7 28.2]
tasmin khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samaye śakro devānāmindro brahmā ca sahāpatiḥ purataḥ sthitāvabhūtām yau bodhisattvaṃ paramagauravajātau divyakāśikavastrāntaritaṃ sarvāṅgapratyaṅgaiḥ smṛtau saṃprajñau pratigṛhṇāte sma | [LalVis, 7 29.1]
yasmiṃśca kūṭāgāre bodhisattvo mātuḥ kukṣigato 'sthāt taṃ brahmā sahāpatirbrahmakāyikāśca devaputrā abhyutkṣipya brahmalokaṃ caityārthaṃ pūjārthaṃ copanāmayāmāsuḥ | [LalVis, 7 30.1]
aparigṛhītaḥ khalu punarbodhisattvaḥ kenacinmanuṣyabhūtena atha tarhi bodhisattvaṃ devatāḥ prathamataraṃ pratigṛhṇanti sma | [LalVis, 7 30.2]
atha bodhisattvo jātamātraḥ pṛthivyāmavatarati sma | [LalVis, 7 31.1]
samanantarāvatīrṇasya ca bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya mahāpṛthivīṃ bhittvā mahāpadmaṃ prādurabhūt | [LalVis, 7 31.2]
nandopanandau ca nāgarājānau gaganatale 'rdhakāyau sthitvā śītoṣṇe dve vāridhāre 'bhinirbhittvā bodhisattvaṃ snāpayataḥ sma | [LalVis, 7 31.3]
śakrabrahmalokapālāḥ pūrvaṃgamāścānye ca bahavo devaputrāḥ śatasahasrā ye bodhisattvaṃ jātamātraṃ nānāgandhodakamuktakusumaiḥ snāpayantyabhyavakiranti sma | [LalVis, 7 31.4]
antarikṣe ca dve cāmare ratnacchatraṃ ca prādurbhūtam | [LalVis, 7 31.5]
sa tasmin mahāpadme sthitvā caturdiśamavalokayati sma | [LalVis, 7 31.6]
caturdiśamavalokya siṃhāvalokitaṃ mahāpuruṣāvalokitaṃ vyavalokayati sma | [LalVis, 7 31.7]
tasmin khalu punaḥ samaye bodhisattvaḥ pūrvakuśalamūlavipākajenāpratihatena divyacakṣuprādurbhūtena divyena cakṣuṣā sarvāvantaṃ trisāhasraṃ mahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātuṃ sanagaranigamajanapadarāṣṭrarājadhānīṃ sadevamānuṣaṃ paśyati sma | [LalVis, 7 32.1]
sarvasattvānāṃ ca cittacaritaṃ ca prajānāti sma | [LalVis, 7 32.2]
jñātvā ca vyavalokayati sma asti tvasau kaścitsattvo yo mayā sadṛśaḥ śīlena vā samādhinā vā prajñayā vā kuśalamūlacaryayā vā | [LalVis, 7 32.3]
yadā ca bodhisattvaḥ trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātau na kaṃcitsattvamātmatulyaṃ paśyati sma atha tasminsamaye bodhisattvaḥ siṃha iva vigatabhayabhairavo 'saṃtrastaḥ astambhī sucintitaṃ smṛtvā cintayitvā sarvasattvānāṃ cittacaritāni jñātvā aparigṛhīto bodhisattvaḥ pūrvāṃ diśamabhimukhaḥ sapta padāni prakrāntaḥ pūrvaṃgamo bhaviṣyāmi sarveṣāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ dharmāṇām | [LalVis, 7 32.4]
tasya prakramata uparyantarīkṣe 'parigṛhītaṃ divyaśvetavipulachatraṃ cāmaraśubhe gacchantamanugacchanti sma yatra yatra ca bodhisattvaḥ padamutkṣipati sma tatra tatra padmāni prādurbhavanti sma | [LalVis, 7 32.5]
dakṣiṇāṃ diśamabhimukhaḥ sapta padāni prakrāntaḥ dakṣiṇīyo bhaviṣyāmi devamanuṣyāṇām | [LalVis, 7 32.6]
paścimāṃ diśamabhimukhaḥ sapta padāni prakrāntaḥ | [LalVis, 7 32.7]
saptame sthitvā siṃha ivāhlādanātmikāṃ vācaṃ bhāṣate sma ahaṃ loke jyeṣṭho 'haṃ loke śreṣṭhaḥ | [LalVis, 7 32.8]
iyaṃ me paścimā jātiḥ | [LalVis, 7 32.9]
kariṣyāmi jātijarāmaraṇaduḥkhasyāntam | [LalVis, 7 32.10]
uttarāṃ diśamabhimukhaḥ sapta padāni prakrāntaḥ anuttaro bhaviṣyāmi sarvasattvānām | [LalVis, 7 32.11]
adhastāddiśamabhimukhaḥ sapta padāni prakrāntaḥ nihaniṣyāmi māraṃ ca mārasenāṃ ca | [LalVis, 7 32.12]
sarvanairayikāṇāṃ ca nirayāgnipratighātāya saha dharmameghavṛṣṭiṃ varṣiṣyāmi yena te sukhasamarpitā bhaviṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 32.13]
upariṣṭāddiśamabhimukhaḥ sapta padāni prakrānta ūrdhvaṃ cāvalokayati sma ullokanīyo bhaviṣyāmi sarvasattvānām | [LalVis, 7 32.14]
samanantarabhāṣitā ceyaṃ bodhisattvena vāk | [LalVis, 7 32.15]
atha tasmin samaye ayaṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātuḥ svareṇābhivijñāpto 'bhūt | [LalVis, 7 32.16]
iyaṃ bodhisattvasya karmavipākajā abhijñādharmatā | [LalVis, 7 32.17]
yadā bodhisattvaścaramabhavika upajāyate yadā cānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyate tadā asyemānyevaṃrūpāṇi ṛddhiprātihāryāṇi bhavanti tasmin khalu punarbhikṣavaḥ samaye saṃhṛṣitaromakūpajātāḥ sarvasattvā abhūvan | [LalVis, 7 33.1]
mahataśca pṛthivīcālasya loke prādurbhāvo 'bhūt bhairavasya romaharṣaṇasya | [LalVis, 7 33.2]
aghaṭṭitāni ca divyamānuṣyakāni tūryāṇi saṃpravāditāni | [LalVis, 7 33.3]
sarvartukālikāśca vṛkṣāstasmin samaye trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātau saṃkusumitāḥ phalitāśca | [LalVis, 7 33.4]
viśuddhācca gaganatalānmeghaśabdaḥ śrūyate sma | [LalVis, 7 33.5]
apagatameghācca gaganācchanaiḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmo devaḥ pravarṣati sma | [LalVis, 7 33.6]
nānāvarṣadivyakusumavastrābharaṇagandhacūrṇavyāmiśrāḥ paramasukhasaṃsparśāśca saumyāḥ sugandhavātāḥ pravāyanti sma | [LalVis, 7 33.7]
vyapagatatamorajodhūmanīhārāśca sarvadiśaḥ suprasannā virājante sma | [LalVis, 7 33.8]
upariṣṭāccāntarikṣādadṛśyā gambhīrā mahābrahmaghoṣāḥ saṃśrūyante sma | [LalVis, 7 33.9]
sarvacandrasūryaśakrabrahmalokapālaprabhāścābhibhūtā abhūvan | [LalVis, 7 33.10]
paramasukhasaṃsparśayā ca sarvasattvakāyacittasukhasaṃjananyā lokottarayā anekaśatasahasravarṇaprabhayā sarvatrisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātuḥ parisphuṭo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 7 33.11]
samantarajātasya khalu punarbodhisattvasyaikāntasukhasamarpitāḥ sarvasattvā babhūvuḥ | [LalVis, 7 33.12]
sarvarāgadveṣamohadarpārativiṣād abhayalobherṣyāmātsaryavigatāḥ sarvākuśalakriyāprativiratā vyādhitānāṃ sattvānāṃ vyādhaya upaśāntāḥ | [LalVis, 7 33.13]
kṣutpipāsitānāṃ sattvānāṃ kṣutpipāsā prasrabdhābhūt | [LalVis, 7 33.14]
madyamadamattānāṃ ca sattvānāṃ madāpagamaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [LalVis, 7 33.15]
unmattaiśca smṛtiḥ pratilabdhā | [LalVis, 7 33.16]
cakṣurvikalaiśca sattvaiścakṣuḥ pratilabdhaṃ śrotravikalaiśca sattvaiḥ śrotram | [LalVis, 7 33.17]
aṅgapratyaṅgavikalendriyāścāvikalendriyāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ | [LalVis, 7 33.18]
daridraiśca dhanāni pratilabdhāni | [LalVis, 7 33.19]
bandhanabaddhāśca bandhanebhyo vimuktāḥ | [LalVis, 7 33.20]
āvīcim ādiṃ kṛtvā sarvanairayikāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ sarvakāraṇād duḥkhaṃ tasminsamaye prasrabdham | [LalVis, 7 33.21]
tiryagyonikānām anyonyabhakṣaṇādi duḥkham yamalokikānāṃ sattvānāṃ kṣutpipāsādiduḥkhaṃ vyupaśāntamabhūt | [LalVis, 7 33.22]
yadā ca bodhisattvo jātamātraḥ sapta padāni prakrānto 'bhūd asaṃkhyeyākalpakoṭinayutaśatasahasraiḥ sucaritacaraṇair mahāvīryamahāsthāmadharmatāpratilambhena tasmin samaye daśadiglokadhātusthitā buddhā bhagavantastaṃ pṛthvīpradeśaṃ vajramayam adhitiṣṭhanti sma | [LalVis, 7 34.1]
yena mahāpṛthivī tasmin pradeśe nāvatīryata tāvanmahābalavegasamanvāgato hi bhikṣavo jātamātro bodhisattvaḥ sapta padāni prakrānto 'bhūt | [LalVis, 7 34.2]
sarvalokāntarikāśca tasmin samaye mahatāvabhāsena sphuṭā abhūvan | [LalVis, 7 34.3]
mahāṃśca tasmin samaye gītaśabdo 'bhūnnṛtyaśabdaḥ | [LalVis, 7 34.4]
aprameyāśca tasmin samaye puṣpacūrṇagandhamālyaratnābharaṇavastrameghā abhipravarṣanti sma | [LalVis, 7 34.5]
paramasukhasamarpitāśca sarvasattvā abhūvan | [LalVis, 7 34.6]
saṃkṣepādacintyā sā kriyābhūd yadā bodhisattvo loke prādurabhūt sarvalokābhyudgataḥ | [LalVis, 7 34.7]
atha khalvāyuṣmānānandaḥ utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇajānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantametadavocat sarvasattvānāṃ bhagavaṃstathāgata āścaryabhūto 'bhūd bodhisattvabhūta evādbhutadharmasamanvāgataśca | [LalVis, 7 35.1]
kaḥ punarvāda evaṃ hyanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ | [LalVis, 7 35.2]
eṣo 'haṃ bhagavaṃścatuṣpañcakṛtvo 'pi daśakṛtvo 'pi yāvatpañcāśatkṛtvo 'pi śatakṛtvo 'pi yāvadanekaśatasahasraśo 'pyahaṃ bhagavan buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi | [LalVis, 7 35.3]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandametadavocat bhaviṣyanti khalu punarānanda anāgate 'dhvani kecidbhikṣavo 'bhāvitakāyā abhāvitacittā abhāvitaśīlā abhāvitaprajñā bālā apaṇḍitā ābhimānikā uddhatā unnatā asaṃvṛtā vikṣiptacittāḥ kāṅkṣāparīttā vicikitsābahulā aśraddhāḥ śramaṇamalāḥ śramaṇapratirūpakāḥ | [LalVis, 7 36.1]
te na śraddhāsyanti imāmevaṃrūpāṃ bodhisattvasya garbhāvakrāntipariśuddhim | [LalVis, 7 36.2]
te 'nyonyamekānte saṃnipātyaivaṃ vakṣyanti paśyata bho yūyam etad apūjyamānaṃ bodhisattvasya kila mātuḥ kukṣigatasyoccāraprasrāvamaṇḍoparimiśrasya īdṛśī vibhūtirāsīt | [LalVis, 7 36.3]
sa ca kila abhiniṣkrāman māturdakṣiṇāyāḥ kukṣer anupalipto garbhamalenābhūditi | [LalVis, 7 36.4]
kathametadyojyate na punaste mohapuruṣā evaṃ jñāsyanti na sukṛtakarmaṇāṃ sattvānāmuccāraprasrāvamaṇḍe kāyaḥ sambhavatīti | [LalVis, 7 36.5]
bhadrikā khalvapi tathārūpāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ garbhāvakrāntirbhavati | [LalVis, 7 36.6]
garbhāvasthitaśca sattvānukampayā hi bodhisattvo manuṣyaloke upapadyate na devabhūta eva dharmacakraṃ pravartayati | [LalVis, 7 36.7]
tatkasmāt mā khalvānanda sattvāḥ kausīdyamāpatsyante | [LalVis, 7 36.8]
devabhūtaḥ sa bhagavān tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho vayaṃ tu manuṣyamātrāḥ | [LalVis, 7 36.9]
na vayaṃ samarthāstatsthānaṃ paripūrayitumiti kausīdyamāpadyeran | [LalVis, 7 36.10]
na khalu punasteṣāṃ mohapuruṣāṇāṃ dharmastainyakānāmevaṃ bhaviṣyati acintyo hi sa sattvo nāsāvasmābhiḥ prāmāṇikaḥ kartavya iti | [LalVis, 7 36.11]
api tu khalvānanda buddharddhiprātihāryamapi te tasmin kāle nāvakalpayiṣyanti kimaṅga punarbodhisattvabhūtasya tathāgatasya bodhisattvaprātihāryāṇi | [LalVis, 7 36.12]
paśya ānanda kiyantaṃ te mohapuruṣā bahvapuṇyābhisaṃskāramabhisaṃskariṣyanti ye buddhadharmān pratikṣepsyanti lābhasatkāraślokābhibhūtā uccāralagnā lābhasatkārābhibhūtā itarajātīyāḥ | [LalVis, 7 36.13]
ānanda āha mā maivaṃrūpā bhagavan anāgate 'dhvani bhikṣavo bhaviṣyanti ya imāmevaṃ bhadrikāṃ sūtrāntāṃ pratikṣepsyanti pratipakṣaṃ pakṣanti ca | [LalVis, 7 37.1]
bhagavānāha evaṃrūpāśca te ānanda sūtrāntāṃ pratikṣepsyanti prativakṣyanti cānekaprakārān cānyān pāpakānabhisaṃskārānabhisaṃskariṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 38.1]
anarthikāśca te śrāmaṇyena bhaviṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 38.2]
ānanda āha kā punarbhagavan teṣāṃ tathārūpāṇāmasatpuruṣāṇāṃ gatirbhaviṣyati ko 'bhisaṃparāyaḥ | [LalVis, 7 39.1]
bhagavānāha yā gatir buddhabodhim antardhāyāpyatītānāgatapratyutpannāṃśca buddhān bhagavato 'tyākhyāya tāṃ te gatiṃ gamiṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 39.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmānānandaḥ saṃharṣitaromakūpajāto namo buddhāya ityuktvā bhagavantametadavocan mūrcchā me bhagavan kāyasyābhūdimaṃ teṣāmasatpuruṣāṇāṃ samudācāraṃ śrutvā | [LalVis, 7 40.1]
bhagavānāha na teṣāmānanda samācāro bhaviṣyati | [LalVis, 7 41.1]
viṣamasamudācārāḥ khalu punaste sattvā bhaviṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 41.2]
te tena viṣamena samudācāreṇāvīcau mahānarake prapatiṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 41.3]
tatkasya hetor ye kecidānanda bhikṣavo vā bhikṣuṇyo vā upāsako vā upāsikā vā imānevaṃrūpān sūtrāntān śrutvā nādhimokṣyanti na śraddhāsyanti na prativetsyanti te cyutāḥ samānā avīcau mahānarake prapatiṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 41.4]
mā ānanda tathāgatāprāmāṇikaṃ akārṣuḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.5]
tatkasmāddhetor aprameyo hyānanda tathāgato gambhīro vipulo duravagāhaḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.6]
yeṣāṃ keṣāṃcidānanda imānevaṃrūpān sūtrāntāñchrutvopapatsyate prītiprāmodyaṃ prasādalābhāstaiḥ sattvaiḥ sulabdhāḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.7]
amoghaṃ ca teṣāṃ jīvitam amoghaṃ ca teṣāṃ mānuṣyaṃ sucaritacaraṇāśca te ādattaṃ ca taiḥ sāraṃ muktāśca te tribhyo 'pāyebhyaḥ bhaviṣyanti ca te putrāstathāgatasya pariprāptaṃ ca taiḥ sarvakāryam amoghaśca teṣāṃ śraddhāpratilambhaḥ suvibhaktaṃ ca tai rāṣṭrapiṇḍaṃ prasannāśca te 'grasattvaiḥ saṃchinnāstairmārapāśāḥ nistīrṇaśca taiḥ saṃsārāṭavīkāntāraḥ samuddhṛtaśca taiḥ śokaśalyo 'nuprāptaṃ ca taiḥ prāmodyavastu sugṛhītāni ca taiḥ śaraṇagamanāni dakṣiṇīyāśca te pūjārhāḥ durlabhaprādurbhāvāśca te loke dakṣiṇīyāśca te dhārayitavyāḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.8]
tatkasya hetos tathā hi te sarvaloke imamevaṃ sarvalokavipratyanīkaṃ tathāgatadharmaṃ śraddadhanti | [LalVis, 7 41.9]
na te ānanda sattvā avarakeṇa kuśalamūlena samanvāgatā bhavanti | [LalVis, 7 41.10]
te cānanda sattvā mamaikajātipratibaddhāni mitrāṇi bhaviṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 41.11]
tatkasmāddhetoḥ kaścidānanda śravaṇādeva priyo bhavati manāpaśca na tu darśanena | [LalVis, 7 41.12]
kaścidānanda darśanenāpi priyo bhavati manāpaśca na tu khalu punaḥ śravaṇena | [LalVis, 7 41.13]
kaścidānanda darśanenāpi śravaṇenāpi priyo bhavati manāpaśca | [LalVis, 7 41.14]
teṣāṃ keṣāṃcidānanda ahaṃ darśanena vā śravaṇena vā priyo manāpo bhaveyaṃ niṣṭhāṃ tvaṃ tatra gacchethāḥ na tāni mamaikajātipratibaddhāni mitrāṇi | [LalVis, 7 41.15]
dṛṣṭāste tathāgatena mocayitavyāste tathāgatena te samaguṇapratyaṃśās te tathāgataguṇapratyaṃśās te tathāgatena kartavyā upāsakāḥ te tathāgataṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā upāttāste tathāgatena | [LalVis, 7 41.16]
mamāntikāt khalvapyānanda pūrvaṃ bodhisattvacaryāmeva tāvaccarato ye kecidbhayārditāḥ sattvā āgatya abhayaṃ pratiyācante sma tebhyo 'haṃ sattvebhyo 'bhayaṃ dattavān kimaṅga punaretarhyanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.17]
śraddhāyāmānanda yogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.18]
idaṃ tathāgato vijñāpayati | [LalVis, 7 41.19]
yadānanda tathāgatena yuṣmākaṃ karaṇīyaṃ kṛtaṃ tattathāgatena śodhito mānaśalyaḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.20]
śravaṇenāpyānanda mitrasya nanu yojanaśatāntaramapi gacchanti gatvā ca sukhitā bhavanti adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ mitraṃ dṛṣṭvā | [LalVis, 7 41.21]
kaḥ punarvādo ye māṃ niśritya kuśalamūlānyavaropayanti | [LalVis, 7 41.22]
jñāsyantyānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ pūrvaṃ mitrāṇyete sattvāstathāgatānām asmākamapyete mitrāṇi bhavantīti | [LalVis, 7 41.23]
tatkasmāt khalu punarānanda mitraṃ mitrasya priyaṃ ca manāpaṃ ca bhavati tasyāpi tadapi priyameva bhavati mitrasya yatpriyaṃ mitram tadapi priyameva bhavati manāpaṃ ca | [LalVis, 7 41.24]
tasmāttarhyānanda ārocayāmi ca prativedayāmi ca | [LalVis, 7 41.25]
śraddhāmātrakamutpādayatha | [LalVis, 7 41.26]
anuparindiṣyāmo vayamanāgatānāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantike te 'smākamapi mitrāṇīti viditvā yathābhiprāyaṃ paripūrayiṣyanti | [LalVis, 7 41.27]
tadyathāpi nāma ānanda kasyacideva puruṣasyaikaputrako bhavet suvayāḥ pradakṣiṇagrāhī | [LalVis, 7 41.28]
sa ca puruṣo bahumitro bhavet | [LalVis, 7 41.29]
sa tasmin pitari kālagate na hi vihanyeta pitṛmitrasuparigṛhītaḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.30]
evameva ānanda ye kecinmama śraddhāsyanti tānahamupādadāmi | [LalVis, 7 41.31]
mitrāṇīva mama tāni | [LalVis, 7 41.32]
te mama śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.33]
bahumitraśca tathāgataḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.34]
tāni ca tathāgatasya mitrāṇi bhūtavādīni na mṛṣāvādīni | [LalVis, 7 41.35]
anuparindāmyahaṃ bhūtavādinām | [LalVis, 7 41.36]
yāni tathāgatasya mitrāṇyanāgatāstathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.37]
śraddhāyāmānanda yogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [LalVis, 7 41.38]
atrāhaṃ yuṣmān vijñāpayāmīti | [LalVis, 7 41.39]
iti hi jāte bodhisattve gaganatalagatānyapsaraḥkoṭinayutaśatasahasrāṇi divyaiḥ puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanavastrābharaṇair māyādevīmabhyavakiranti sma | [LalVis, 7 42.1]
tatredamucyate | [LalVis, 7 42.2]
iti hi bhikṣavo jāte bodhisattve tatkṣaṇaṃ dānanisargaḥ punaruttari pravartate sma | [LalVis, 7 67.1]
pañca ca kulikāśatāni prasūyante sma daśa ca kanyāsahasrāṇi yaśovatīpramukhāni | [LalVis, 7 67.2]
aṣṭau dāsīśatāni aṣṭau dāsaśatāni chandakapramukhāni | [LalVis, 7 67.3]
daśa vaḍavāsahasrāṇi daśa kiśorasahasrāṇi kaṇṭhakapramukhāni | [LalVis, 7 67.4]
pañca kareṇusahasrāṇi pañca piṅgasahasrāṇi prasūyante sma | [LalVis, 7 67.5]
tāni sarvāṇi rājñā śuddhodanena pustavaropitāni kumārasya krīḍārthaṃ dattānyabhūvan | [LalVis, 7 67.6]
caturṇāṃ ca dvīpakoṭīśatasahasrāṇāṃ madhye pṛthivīpradeśe aśvatthayaṣṭiḥ prādurabhūdantardvīpe ca candanavanaṃ prādurbabhūva bodhisattvasya paribhogārthaṃ bodhisattvasyaivānubhāvena | [LalVis, 7 68.1]
pañca codyānaśatāni samantānnagarasya prādurbabhūvurbodhisattvasya paribhogāya | [LalVis, 7 68.2]
pañca ca nidhānasahasrāṇi dharaṇītalādutplutya mukhaṃ darśayanti sma | [LalVis, 7 68.3]
iti hi ye kecidrājñaḥ śuddhodanasyārthābhipretā abhūvan te sarve samṛddhābhipretā abhūvan saṃsiddhāḥ | [LalVis, 7 68.4]
tato rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyaitadabhūt kimahaṃ kumārasya nāmadheyaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [LalVis, 7 69.1]
tato 'syaitadabhūd asya hi jātamātreṇa mama sarvārthāḥ saṃsiddhāḥ | [LalVis, 7 69.2]
yannvahamasya sarvārthasiddha iti nāma kuryām | [LalVis, 7 69.3]
tato rājā bodhisattvaṃ mahatā satkāreṇa satkṛtya sarvārthasiddho 'yaṃ kumāro nāmnā bhavatu iti nāmāsyākārṣīt | [LalVis, 7 69.4]
iti hi bhikṣavo jāte bodhisattve mātuḥ kukṣipārśvamakṣatamanupahatamabhavadyathā pūrvaṃ tathā paścāt | [LalVis, 7 70.1]
tritaviṣyandāmbukūpāḥ prādurabhūvan api ca sugandhatailapuṣkariṇyaḥ | [LalVis, 7 70.2]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyagandhaparivāsitatailaparigṛhītāni bodhisattvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.3]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyānulepanaparigṛhītāni bodhisattvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.4]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyagandhodakaparipūrṇaghaṭāparigṛhītāni bodhisattvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.5]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyānulepanaparigṛhītāni bodhisattvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.6]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyadārakācīvaraparigṛhītāni bodhisatvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.7]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyadārakābharaṇaparigṛhītāni bodhisattvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.8]
pañcāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi divyatūryasaṃgītisaṃprabhaṇitena bodhisattvamātaramupasaṃkramya sujātajāte tāmaklāntakāyatāṃ ca paripṛcchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.9]
yāvantaśceha jambudvīpe bāhyāḥ pañcābhijñā ṛṣayaste sarve gaganatalenāgatya rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya purataḥ sthitvā jayavṛddhiśabdamanuśrāvayanti sma | [LalVis, 7 70.10]
iti hi bhikṣavo jātamātro bodhisattvaḥ saptarātraḥ lumbinīvane divyamānuṣyakaistūryatālāvacaraiḥ satkriyate sma gurukriyate sma mānyate sma pūjyate sma khādyabhojyasvādanīyāni viśrāṇyante sma | [LalVis, 7 71.1]
sarvaśākyagaṇāśca saṃnipātyānandaśabdamudīrayanti sma dānāni ca dadanti sma puṇyāni ca kurvanti sma | [LalVis, 7 71.2]
dvātriṃśacca brāhmaṇaśatasahasrāṇi dine dine saṃtarpyante sma | [LalVis, 7 71.3]
yeṣāṃ ca yenārthena tebhyastaddīyate sma | [LalVis, 7 71.4]
śakraśca devānāmindro brahmā ca tasyāṃ brāhmaṇaparṣadi māṇavakarūpamabhinirmāyāgrāsane niṣadyemāṃ maṅgalyāṃ gāthāmabhyabhāṣatām | [LalVis, 7 71.5]
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ saptarātrajātasya bodhisattvasya mātā māyādevī kālamakarot | [LalVis, 7 82.1]
sā kālagatā trāyatriṃśati deveṣūpapadyata | [LalVis, 7 82.2]
syāt khalu punarbhikṣavo yuṣmākamevaṃ bodhisattvāparādhena māyādevī kālagateti na khalvevaṃ draṣṭavyam | [LalVis, 7 82.3]
tatkasmāddhetor etat paramaṃ hi tasyā āyuṣpramāṇamabhūt | [LalVis, 7 82.4]
atītānāmapi bhikṣavo bodhisattvānāṃ saptarātrajātānāṃ janetryaḥ kālamakurvanta | [LalVis, 7 82.5]
tatkasmāddhetoḥ vivṛddhasya hi bodhisattvasya paripūrṇendriyasyābhiniṣkrāmato māturhṛdayaṃ sphuṭet | [LalVis, 7 82.6]
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ saptame divase yādṛśenaiva vyūhena māyādevī kapilavastuno mahānagarādudyānabhūmimabhiniṣkrāntābhūt tataḥ koṭīśatasahasraguṇottareṇa mahāvyūhena bodhisattvaḥ kapilavastu mahānagaraṃ prāvikṣat | [LalVis, 7 83.1]
tasya ca praviśataḥ pañca pūrṇakumbhasahasrāṇi gandhodakaparipūrṇāni purato nīyante sma | [LalVis, 7 83.2]
evaṃ pañcakanyāsahasrāṇi mayūrahastakaparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.3]
pañca ca kanyāsahasrāṇi tālavṛkṣakaparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.4]
pañca sa kanyāsahasrāṇi gandhodakabhṛṅgāraparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma mārgamavasiñcanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.5]
pañca ca kanyāsahasrāṇi vicitrapaṭalakaparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.6]
pañca ca kanyāsahasrāṇi navavicitrapralambanamālāparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.7]
pañca ca kanyāsahasrāṇi ratnabhadrālaṃkāraparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma mārgaṃ śodhayanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.8]
pañca ca kanyāsahasrāṇi bhadrāsanaparigṛhītāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.9]
pañca ca brāhmaṇasahasrāṇi ghaṇṭāparigṛhītāni māṅgalyaśabdaṃ śrāvayantaḥ purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.10]
viṃśatināgasahasrāṇi sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.11]
viṃśatihayasahasrāṇi suvarṇālaṃkārasaṃchannāni sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitāni purato gacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.12]
aśītirathasahasrāṇi ucchritachatradhvajapatākākiṅkiṇījālasamalaṃkṛtāni bodhisattvasya pṛṣṭhato 'nugacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.13]
catvāriṃśatpadātisahasrāṇi śūrāṇāṃ vīrāṇāṃ varāṅgarūpiṇāṃ saṃnaddhadṛḍhavarmakavacānāṃ bodhisattvaṃ gacchantamanugacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.14]
gaganatalagatāni cāprameyāsaṃkhyeyānyabhijñātāni kāmāvacarāṇāṃ rūpāvacaradevaputrakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi nānāprakāram anekavyūhair bodhisattvasya pūjāṃ kurvanto 'nugacchanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.15]
yasmiṃśca varapravararathe bodhisattvaḥ samabhirūḍho 'bhūt sa kāmāvacarairdevair anekairmahāvyūhaiḥ samalaṃkṛto 'bhūt | [LalVis, 7 83.16]
viṃśati ca devakanyāsahasrāṇi sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitāni ratnasūtraparigṛhītāni taṃ rathaṃ vahanti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.17]
dvayoścāpsarasormadhye ekā mānuṣī kanyā dvayormānuṣīkanyayormadhye ekāpsarā | [LalVis, 7 83.18]
na cāpsaraso mānuṣīṇāmāmagandhaṃ jighranti sma | [LalVis, 7 83.19]
na ca mānuṣā apsarasāṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā pramādamāpadyante sma yadidaṃ bodhisattvasya tejo'nubhāvena | [LalVis, 7 83.20]
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ kapilāhvaye puravare sarvārthasiddhāya pañcamātraiḥ śākyaśataiḥ pañcagṛhaśatāni nirmāpitānyabhūvan bodhisattvamuddiśya | [LalVis, 7 84.1]
te bodhisattvaṃ nagaraṃ praviśantaṃ svasvagṛhadvāramūle sthitvā kṛtāñjalipuṭā abhinatakāyāḥ sagauravā evamāhur iha bhoḥ sarvārthasiddha praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.2]
iha bho devātideva praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.3]
iha bhoḥ śuddhasattva praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.4]
iha bhoḥ sārathivara praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.5]
iha bhoḥ prītiprāmodyakara praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.6]
iha bho aninditayaśaḥ praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.7]
iha bhoḥ samantacakṣu praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.8]
iha bho asamasama praviśa | [LalVis, 7 84.9]
iha bho asadṛśaguṇatejodhara lakṣaṇānuvyañjanasvalaṃkṛtakāya praviśeti | [LalVis, 7 84.10]
tataścopādāya kumārasyeha sarvārthasiddhaḥ sarvārthasiddha iti saṃjñāmagamat | [LalVis, 7 84.11]
tatra rājā śuddhodanasteṣāṃ sarveṣāmanuvartanārthaṃ bodhisattvaṃ sarvagṛheṣu praveśya caturṇāṃ māsānāmatyayādbodhisattvaṃ svagṛhe praveśayati sma | [LalVis, 7 85.1]
tatra ca nānāratnavyūho nāma mahāprāsādastaṃ bodhisattvaḥ samārūḍho 'bhūt | [LalVis, 7 85.2]
tatra te vṛddhavṛddhāḥ śākyāḥ saṃnipatyaivaṃ mataṃ cārayanti sma kā nu khalu samarthā bodhisattvaṃ gopāyituṃ kelayituṃ mamāyituṃ hitacittatayā maitracittatayā guṇacittatayā saumyacittatayā ceti | [LalVis, 7 85.3]
tatra pañcamātrāṇi śākyavadhūśatāni | [LalVis, 7 85.4]
ekaikā evamāhur ahaṃ kumāramupasthāsya iti | [LalVis, 7 85.5]
tatra mahallakamahallikāḥ śākyā evamāhuḥ sarvā etā vadhūkā navā dahrāstaruṇyaḥ rūpayauvanamadamattāḥ | [LalVis, 7 85.6]
naitāḥ samarthā bodhisattvaṃ kālena kālamupasthāpayitum | [LalVis, 7 85.7]
atha ca punariyaṃ mahāprajāpatī gautamī kumārasya mātṛsvasā | [LalVis, 7 85.8]
eṣā samarthā kumāraṃ samyaksukhena saṃvardhayitum rājānaṃ ca śuddhodanamabhidhārayitum | [LalVis, 7 85.9]
iti hi te sarve samagrā bhūtvā mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīmutsāhayanti sma | [LalVis, 7 85.10]
iti hi mahāprajāpatī gautamī kumāraṃ saṃvardhayati sma | [LalVis, 7 85.11]
tatra bodhisattvasyārthe dvātriṃśaddhātryaḥ saṃsthāpitā abhuvan aṣṭāvaṅgadhātryaḥ aṣṭau kṣīradhātryaḥ aṣṭau maladhātryaḥ aṣṭau krīḍādhātryaḥ | [LalVis, 7 85.12]
tato rājā śuddhodanaḥ sarvaṃ śākyagaṇaṃ saṃnipātyaivaṃ mīmāṃsate sma kiṃ nu khalvayaṃ kumāro rājā bhaviṣyati cakravartī āhosvid abhiniṣkramiṣyati pravrajyāyai | [LalVis, 7 86.1]
tena ca samayena himavataḥ parvatarājasya pārśve asito nāma maharṣiḥ prativasati sma pañcābhijñaḥ sārdhaṃ naradattena bhāgineyena | [LalVis, 7 86.2]
sa bodhisattvasya jātamātrasya bahūnyāścaryādbhutaprātihāryāṇyadrākṣīt | [LalVis, 7 86.3]
gaganatalagatāṃśca devaputrān buddhaśabdamanuśrāvayato 'mbarāṇi ca bhrāmayata itastataḥ pramuditān bhramato 'drākṣīt | [LalVis, 7 86.4]
tasyaitadabhūd yannvahaṃ vyavalokayeyamiti | [LalVis, 7 86.5]
sa divyena cakṣuṣā sarvaṃ jambudvīpamanuvilokayannadrākṣīt kapilāhvaye mahāpuravare rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhe kumāraṃ jātaṃ śatapuṇyatejastejitaṃ sarvalokamahitaṃ dvātriṃśanmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtagātram | [LalVis, 7 86.6]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarnaradattaṃ māṇavakamāmantrayate sma yat khalu māṇavaka jānīyā jambudvīpe mahāratnamutpannam | [LalVis, 7 86.7]
kapilavastuni mahānagare rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhe kumāro jātaḥ śatapuṇyatejastejitaḥ sarvalokamahito dvātriṃśanmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samanvāgataḥ | [LalVis, 7 86.8]
sacetso 'gāramadhyāvasiṣyati rājā bhaviṣyati caturaṅgaścakravartī vijitavān dhārmiko dharmarājo jānapadasthāmavīryaprāptaḥ saptaratnasamanvāgataḥ | [LalVis, 7 86.9]
tasyemāni sapta ratnāni bhavanti | [LalVis, 7 86.10]
tadyathā cakraratnaṃ hastiratnaṃ aśvaratnaṃ maṇiratnaṃ strīratnaṃ gṛhapatiratnaṃ pariṇāyakaratnam | [LalVis, 7 86.11]
evaṃ saptaratnasampūrṇaśca | [LalVis, 7 86.12]
asya putrasahasraṃ bhaviṣyati śūrāṇāṃ vīrāṇāṃ varāṅgarūpiṇāṃ parasainyapramardakānām | [LalVis, 7 86.13]
sa imaṃ mahāpṛthivīmaṇḍalaṃ samudraparikhamadaṇḍenāśastreṇa svena dharmeṇa balenābhibhūyābhinirjitya rājyaṃ kariṣyatyaiśvaryādhipatyena | [LalVis, 7 86.14]
sacetpunaragārādanagārikāṃ pravrajiṣyati tathāgato bhaviṣyati arhan samyaksaṃbuddho netā ananyaneyaḥ śāstā loke saṃbuddhaḥ | [LalVis, 7 86.15]
tadetarhyupasaṃkramiṣyāvastad draṣṭumiti | [LalVis, 7 86.16]
atha khalvasito maharṣiḥ sārdhaṃ naradattena bhāgineyena rājahaṃsa iva gaganatalādabhyudgamya samutplutya yena kapilavastu mahānagaraṃ tenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 7 87.1]
upasaṃkramya ṛddhiṃ pratisaṃhṛtya padbhyāmeva kapilavastu mahānagaraṃ praviśya yena rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 7 87.2]
upasaṃkramya rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhadvāre 'sthāt | [LalVis, 7 87.3]
iti hi bhikṣavo 'sito maharṣiḥ paśyati sma rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya gṛhadvāre 'nekāni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi saṃnipatitāni | [LalVis, 7 88.1]
atha khalvasito maharṣirdauvārikamupasaṃkramyaivamāha gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya nivedaya dvāre ṛṣirvyavasthita iti | [LalVis, 7 88.2]
parameti dauvāriko 'sitasya maharṣeḥ pratiśrutya yena rājā śuddhodanastenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 7 88.3]
upasaṃkramya kṛtāñjalipuṭo rājānaṃ śuddhodanamevamāha yat khalu deva jānīyā ṛṣirjīrṇo vṛddho mahallako dvāre sthitaḥ | [LalVis, 7 88.4]
evaṃ ca vadati rājānamahaṃ draṣṭukāma iti | [LalVis, 7 88.5]
atha rājā śuddhodano 'sitasya maharṣerāsanaṃ prajñāpya taṃ puruṣamevamāha praviśatu ṛṣiriti | [LalVis, 7 88.6]
atha sa puruṣo rājakulānniṣkramyāsitaṃ maharṣimevamāha praviśeti | [LalVis, 7 88.7]
atha khalvasito maharṣiryena rājā śuddhodanastenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 7 89.1]
upasaṃkramya purataḥ sthitvā rājānaṃ śuddhodanamevamāha jaya jaya mahārāja ciramāyuḥ pālaya dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayeti | [LalVis, 7 89.2]
atha sa rājā śuddhodano 'sitasya maharṣerarghapādyamarcanaṃ ca kṛtvā sādhu suṣṭhu ca parigṛhya āsanenopanimantrayate sma | [LalVis, 7 90.1]
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ cainaṃ jñātvā sagauravaḥ supratīta evamāha na smarāmyahaṃ tava ṛṣe darśanam | [LalVis, 7 90.2]
tatkenārthenehābhyāgato 'si kiṃ prayojanam | [LalVis, 7 90.3]
evamukte 'sito maharṣī rājānaṃ śuddhodanametadavocat putraste mahārāja jātastamahaṃ draṣṭukāma ihāgata iti | [LalVis, 7 90.4]
rājā āha svapiti maharṣe kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 91.1]
muhūrtamāgamaya yāvadutthāsyatīti | [LalVis, 7 91.2]
ṛṣiravocan na mahārāja tādṛśā mahāpuruṣāściraṃ svapanti | [LalVis, 7 92.1]
jāgaraśīlāstādṛśāḥ satpuruṣā bhavanti | [LalVis, 7 92.2]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo 'sitasya maharṣeranukampayā jāgaraṇanimittamakarot | [LalVis, 7 93.1]
atha khalu rājā śuddhodanaḥ sarvārthasiddhaṃ kumāramubhābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ sādhu ca suṣṭhu cānuparigṛhya asitasya maharṣerantikamupanāmayati sma | [LalVis, 7 93.2]
iti hi asito maharṣirbodhisattvamavalokya dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samanvāgatamaśītyanuvyañjanasuvicitragātraṃ śakrabrahmalokapālātirekavapuṣaṃ dinakaraśatasahasrātirekatejasaṃ sarvāṅgasundaraṃ dṛṣṭvā codānamudānayati sma āścaryapudgalo batāyaṃ loke prādurbhūta mahāścaryapudgalo batāyaṃ loke prādurbhūta ityutthāyāsanātkṛtāñjalipuṭo bodhisattvasya caraṇayoḥ praṇipatya pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca bodhisattvamaṅkena parigṛhya nidhyāyannavasthito 'bhūt | [LalVis, 7 94.1]
so 'drākṣīdbodhisattvasya dvātriṃśanmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇāni yaiḥ samanvāgatasya puruṣapudgalasya dve gatī bhavato nānyā | [LalVis, 7 94.2]
sacedagāramadhyāvasati rājā bhavati caturaṅgaścakravartī pūrvavadyāvadevaiśvaryādhipatyena | [LalVis, 7 94.3]
sacetpunaragārādanagārikāṃ pravrajati tathāgato bhaviṣyati vighuṣṭaśabdaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [LalVis, 7 94.4]
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā prārodīdaśrūṇi ca pravartayan gambhīraṃ ca niśvasati sma | [LalVis, 7 94.5]
adrākṣīdrājā śuddhodano 'sitaṃ maharṣiṃ rudantamaśrūṇi ca pravartayamānaṃ gambhīraṃ ca niśvasantam | [LalVis, 7 95.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca saṃharṣitaromakūpajātastvaritatvaritaṃ dīnamanā asitaṃ maharṣimetadavocat kimidamṛṣe rodasi aśrūṇi ca pravartayasi gambhīraṃ ca niśvasasi mā khalu kumārasya kācidvipratipattiḥ | [LalVis, 7 95.2]
evamukte 'sito maharṣī rājānaṃ śuddhodanamevamāha nāhaṃ mahārāja kumārasyārthena rodimi nāpyasya kācidvipratipattiḥ | [LalVis, 7 96.1]
kiṃtvātmānamahaṃ rodimi | [LalVis, 7 96.2]
tatkasmāddhetor ahaṃ ca mahārāja jīrṇo vṛddho mahallakaḥ | [LalVis, 7 96.3]
ayaṃ ca sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāro 'vaśyamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyati | [LalVis, 7 96.4]
abhisaṃbudhya cānuttaraṃ dharmacakraṃ pravartayiṣyati apravartitaṃ śramaṇena vā brāhmaṇena vā devena vā māreṇa vā anyena vā punaḥ kenacilloke sahadharmeṇa | [LalVis, 7 96.5]
sadevakasya lokasya hitāya sukhāya dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati ādau kalyāṇaṃ madhye kalyāṇaṃ paryavasāne kalyāṇam | [LalVis, 7 96.6]
svarthaṃ suvyañjanaṃ kevalaṃ paripūrṇaṃ pariśuddhaṃ paryavadātaṃ brahmacaryaṃ sattvānāṃ saṃprakāśayiṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.7]
asmāttaṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā jātidharmāṇaḥ sattvā jātyā parimokṣante | [LalVis, 7 96.8]
evaṃ jarāvyādhimaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsebhyaḥ parimokṣante | [LalVis, 7 96.9]
rāgadveṣamohāgnisaṃtaptānāṃ sattvānāṃ saddharmajalavarṣeṇa prahlādanaṃ kariṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.10]
nānākudṛṣṭigrahaṇapraskandhānāṃ sattvānāṃ kupathaprayātānāmṛjumārgeṇa nirvāṇapathamupaneṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.11]
saṃsārapañjaracārakāvaruddhānāṃ kleśabandhanabaddhānāṃ bandhananirmokṣaṃ kariṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.12]
ajñānatamastimirapaṭalaparyavanaddhanayanānāṃ sattvānāṃ prajñācakṣurutpādayiṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.13]
kleśaśalyaviddhānāṃ sattvānāṃ śalyoddharaṇaṃ kariṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.14]
tadyathā mahārāja audumbarapuṣpaṃ kadācitkarhicilloke utpadyate evameva mahārāja kadācitkarhicidbahubhiḥ kalpakoṭinayutairbuddhā bhagavanto loke utpadyante | [LalVis, 7 96.15]
so 'yaṃ kumāro 'vaśyamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [LalVis, 7 96.16]
abhisaṃbudhya ca sattvakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi saṃsārasāgarāt pāramuttārayiṣyati amṛte ca pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyati | [LalVis, 7 96.17]
vayaṃ ca taṃ buddharatnaṃ na drakṣyāmaḥ | [LalVis, 7 96.18]
ityeva tadahaṃ mahārāja rodimi paridīnamanā dīrghaṃ ca niśvasāmi yadahamimaṃ nārogye 'pi rādhayiṣyāmi | [LalVis, 7 96.19]
yathā hyasmākaṃ mahārāja mantravedaśāstreṣvāgacchati nārhati sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāro 'gāram adhyāvasitum | [LalVis, 7 97.1]
tatkasya hetos tathā hi mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāro dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samanvāgataḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.2]
katamairdvātriṃśatā tadyathā | [LalVis, 7 97.3]
uṣṇīṣaśīrṣo mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.4]
anena mahārāja prathamena mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇena samanvāgataḥ sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.5]
bhinnāñjanamayūrakalāpābhinīlavallitapradakṣiṇāvartakeśaḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.6]
samavipulalalāṭaḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.7]
ūrṇā mahārāja sarvārthasiddhasya kumārasya bhruvormadhye jātā himarajataprakāśā | [LalVis, 7 97.8]
gopakṣmanetraḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.9]
abhinīlanetraḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.10]

aviraladantaḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.12]

brahmasvaro mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.14]
rasarasāgravān | [LalVis, 7 97.15]
prabhūtatanujihvaḥ | [LalVis, 7 97.16]

dīrghāṅguliradhaḥkramatalayormahārāja sarvārthasiddhasya kumārasya cakre jāte ci arciṣmatī prabhāsvare site sahasrāre sanemike sanābhike | [LalVis, 7 97.35]

saṃvidyante khalu punarmahārāja sarvārthasiddhasya kumārasya kāye 'śītyanuvyañjanāni yaiḥ samanvāgataḥ sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāro nārhatyagāramadhyāvasitum | [LalVis, 7 98.1]
avaśyamabhiniṣkramiṣyati pravrajyāyai | [LalVis, 7 98.2]
katamāni ca mahārāja tānyaśītyanuvyañjanāni tadyathā tuṅganakhaśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.3]
tāmranakhaśca snigdhanakhaśca vṛttāṅguliśca anupūrvacitrāṅguliśca gūḍhaśiraśca gūḍhagulphaśca ghanasaṃdhiśca aviṣamasamapādaśca āyatapārṣṇiśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.4]
snigdhapāṇilekhaśca tulyapāṇilekhaśca gambhīrapāṇilekhaśca ajihmapāṇilekhaśca anupūrvapāṇilekhaśca bimboṣṭhaśca noccavacanaśabdaśca mṛdutaruṇatāmrajihvaśca gajagarjitābhistanitameghasvaramadhuramañjughoṣaśca paripūrṇavyañjanaśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.5]
pralambabāhuśca śucigātravastusampannaśca mṛdugātraśca viśālagātraśca adīnagātraśca anupūrvonnatagātraśca susamāhitagātraśca suvibhaktagātraśca pṛthuvipulasuparipūrṇajānumaṇḍalaśca vṛttagātraśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.6]
suparimṛṣṭagātraśca ajihmavṛṣabhagātraśca anupūrvagātraśca gambhīranābhiśca ajihmanābhiśca anupūrvanābhiśca śucyācāraśca ṛṣabhavat samantaprāsādikaśca paramasuviśuddhavitimirālokasamantaprabhaśca nāgavilambitagatiśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.7]
siṃhavikrāntagatiśca ṛṣabhavikrāntagatiśca haṃsavikrāntagatiśca abhipradakṣiṇāvartagatiśca vṛttakukṣiśca mṛṣṭakukṣiśca ajihmakukṣiśca cāpodaraśca vyapagatachandadoṣanīlakālakāduṣṭaśarīraśca vṛttadaṃṣṭraśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.8]
tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraśca anupūrvadaṃṣṭraśca tuṅganāsaśca śucinayanaśca vimalanayanaśca prahasitanayanaśca āyatanayanaśca viśālanayanaśca nīlakuvalayadalasadṛśanayanaśca sahitabhrūśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.9]
citrabhrūśca asitabhrūśca saṃgatabhrūśca anupūrvabhrūśca pīnagaṇḍaśca aviṣamagaṇḍaśca vyapagatagaṇḍadoṣaśca anupahatakruṣṭaśca suviditendriyaśca suparipūrṇendriyaśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.10]
saṃgatamukhalalāṭaśca paripūrṇottamāṅgaśca asitakeśaśca sahitakeśaśca susaṃgatakeśaśca surabhikeśaśca aparuṣakeśaśca anākulakeśaśca anupūrvakeśaśca sukuñcitakeśaśca śrīvatsasvastikanandyāvartavardhamānasaṃsthānakeśaśca mahārāja sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 7 98.11]
imāni tāni mahārāja sarvārthasiddhasya kumārasyāśītyanuvyañjanāni yaiḥ samanvāgataḥ sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāro nārhatyagāramadhyāvasitum | [LalVis, 7 98.12]
avaśyamabhiniṣkramiṣyati pravrajyāyai | [LalVis, 7 98.13]
atha khalu rājā śuddhodano 'sitasya maharṣeḥ sakāśātkumārasyedaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ śrutvā saṃtuṣṭa udagra āttamanāḥ pramuditaḥ prītisaumanasyajāta utthāyāsanādbodhisattvasya caraṇayoḥ praṇipatyemāṃ gāthāmabhāṣata | [LalVis, 7 99.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo rājā śuddhodano 'sitaṃ maharṣiṃ sārdhaṃ naradattena bhāgineyenānurūpeṇa bhaktena saṃtarpayati sma | [LalVis, 7 101.1]
saṃtarpyābhicchādya pradakṣiṇamakarot | [LalVis, 7 101.2]
atha khalvasito maharṣistata evarddhyā vihāyasā prākramat yena svāśramastenopāsaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 7 101.3]
atha khalu dvayaṃ saṃkramya tatra khalvasito maharṣirnaradattaṃ māṇavakametadavocad yadā tvaṃ naradatta śṛṇuyā buddho loke utpanna iti tadā tvaṃ gatvā tasya śāsane pravrajeḥ | [LalVis, 7 102.1]
tatte bhaviṣyati dīrgharātramarthāya hitāya sukhāyeti | [LalVis, 7 102.2]
tatredamucyate | [LalVis, 7 103.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo jātamātrasya bodhisattvasya maheśvaro devaputraḥ śuddhāvāsakāyikān devaputrānāmantryaivamāha yo 'sau mārṣā asaṃkhyeyakalpakoṭiniyutaśatasahasrasukṛtakarmadānaśīlakṣāntivīryadhyānaprajñopāyaśrattacaraṇavratatapaḥsucaritacaraṇaḥ mahāmaitrīmahākaruṇāmahāmuditāsamanvāgata upekṣāsamudgatacittaḥ sarvasattvahitasukhodyato dṛḍhavīryakavacasusaṃnāhasaṃnaddhaḥ pūrvajinakṛtakuśalamūloditaḥ śatapuṇyalakṣaṇasamalaṃkṛtaḥ sukṛtaniścayaparākramaḥ paracakrapramathanaḥ suvimalaśuddhāśayasampannaḥ sucaritacaraṇo mahājñānaketudhvajaḥ mārabalāntakaraṇaḥ trisāhasramahāsāhasrasārthavāhaḥ devamanuṣyapūjitamahāyajñayaṣṭaḥ susamṛddhapuṇyanicayaniḥsaraṇābhiprāyo jātijarāmaraṇāntakaraḥ sujātajātaḥ ikṣvākurājakulasambhūto jagadvibodhayitā bodhisattvo mahāsattvo manuṣyaloka upapannaḥ | [LalVis, 7 124.1]
na cirādasāvanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [LalVis, 7 124.2]
hanta gacchāmastamabhivandituṃ mānayituṃ pūjayitum abhistotum anyeṣāṃ ca mānābhibhūtānāṃ devaputrāṇāṃ mānamadadarpacchedanārtham | [LalVis, 7 124.3]
te 'smānabhivandamānān dṛṣṭvā te 'pi bodhisattvaṃ vandiṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti ca | [LalVis, 7 124.4]
tatteṣāṃ bhaviṣyati dīrgharātramarthāya hitāya sukhāya yāvadamṛtādhigamāya | [LalVis, 7 124.5]
rājñaśca śuddhodanasya jayavṛddhiranuśrāvitā bhaviṣyati | [LalVis, 7 124.6]
tattvavyākaraṇena ca bodhisattvaṃ vyākṛtya punarapyāgamiṣyāma iti | [LalVis, 7 124.7]
atha khalu maheśvaro devaputro dvādaśabhirdevaputraśatasahasraiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛtaḥ sarvakapilavastumahānagaramavabhāsena sphurayitvā yena rājñaḥ śuddhodanasya niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 7 125.1]
upasaṃkramya dauvārike nivedya rājñābhyanujñāto rājakulaṃ praviśya bodhisattvasya pādau śirasābhivandyaikāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā anekaśatasahasrakṛtvaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bodhisattvamaṅke samāropya rājānaṃ śuddhodanamāśvāsayati sma tuṣṭo mahārāja bhava paramaprītaśca | [LalVis, 7 125.2]
tatkasmāddhetor yathā mahārāja bodhisattvasya lakṣaṇairanuvyañjanaiśca kāyaḥ samalaṃkṛto yathā ca kumāro 'bhibhavati sadevamānuṣāsuralokaṃ varṇena tejasā ca yaśasā lakṣmyā ca niḥsaṃśayaṃ mahārāja bodhisattvo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [LalVis, 7 125.3]
iti hi bhikṣavo maheśvaro devaputraḥ sārdhaṃ śuddhāvāsakāyikairdevaputrair bodhisattvasya mahatpūjopasthānaṃ kṛtvā bodhisattvaṃ tattvavyākaraṇena vyākṛtya punarapi svabhavanaṃ prākrāmat | [LalVis, 7 126.1]
tatredamucyate | [LalVis, 7 127.1]
{LalVis, 8}
iti hi bhikṣavo yāmeva rātriṃ bodhisattvo jātastasyāmeva rātryāṃ viṃśatikanyāsahasrāṇi kṣatriyabrāhmaṇanaigamagṛhapatimahāśālakuleṣu jātāḥ | [LalVis, 8 1.1]

tadā ca bhikṣavo mahallakamahallikāḥ śākyāḥ saṃnipatya rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramyaivamāhur yatkhalu deva jānīyāḥ devakulaṃ kumāra upanīyatāmiti | [LalVis, 8 2.1]
rājā āha sādhu upanīyatāṃ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 8 2.2]
tena hi maṇḍyatāṃ nagaram | [LalVis, 8 2.3]
