tato rājā śuddhodanaḥ svagṛhaṃ praviśya mahāprajāpatīṃ gautamīmāmantryaivamāha alaṃkriyantāṃ kumāraḥ devakulamupaneṣyata iti | [LalVis, 8 3.1]
sādhviti pratiśrutya mahāprajāpatī gautamī kumāraṃ maṇḍayati sma | [LalVis, 8 3.2]
tataḥ kumāro maṇḍyamānaḥ prahasitavadano vyapagatabhṛkuṭikaḥ paramamadhurayā vācā mātṛsvasāramevamāha amba kutrāhamupaneṣyata iti | [LalVis, 8 4.1]
āha devakulaṃ putreti | [LalVis, 8 4.2]
tataḥ kumāraḥ smitamupadarśayan prahasitavadano mātṛsvasāraṃ gāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [LalVis, 8 4.3]
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ sarvairvarṇaiḥ stutimaṅgalaiḥ pratyupasthitairaparimitālaṃkārālaṃkṛteṣu vīthicatvaraśṛṅgāṭakāntarāpaṇamukheṣvantaḥpure kumārasya rathamalaṃkṛtya rājā śuddhodano brāhmaṇanaigamaśreṣṭhigṛhapatyamātyakoṭṭarājadauvārikapāriṣadyamitrajñātiparivṛtaḥ puraskṛto dhūpanadhūpitena muktapuṣpābhikīrṇena hayagajarathapattikalilenocchritachatradhvajapatākena nānātūryasaṃpravāditena mārgeṇa kumāraṃ gṛhītvā gacchati sma | [LalVis, 8 8.1]
devatāśatasahasrāṇi bodhisattvasya rathaṃ vahanti sma | [LalVis, 8 8.2]
anekāni ca devaputrāpsaraḥkoṭiniyutaśatasahasrāṇi gaganatalagatāni puṣpavarṣāṇyabhipravarṣanti sma | [LalVis, 8 8.3]
tūryāṇi ca pravādayanti sma | [LalVis, 8 8.4]
iti hi rājā śuddhodano mahatā rājavyūhena mahatā rājarddhyā mahatā rājānubhāvena kumāraṃ gṛhītvā devakulaṃ praviśati sma | [LalVis, 8 8.5]
samanantarapratiṣṭhāpitaśca bodhisattvena dakṣiṇaścaraṇayoḥ kramatalastasmin devakule atha tā acetanyo devapratimāḥ tadyathā śivaskandanārāyaṇakuberacandrasūryavaiśravaṇaśakrabrahmalokapālaprabhṛtayaḥ pratimāḥ sarvāḥ svebhyaḥ svebhyaḥ sthānebhyo vyutthāya bodhisattvasya kramatalayornipatanti sma | [LalVis, 8 8.6]
tatra devamanuṣyaśatasahasrāṇi hīhīkārakilakilāpramukhaiḥ prakṣveḍitaśatasahasrāṇi prāmuñcan | [LalVis, 8 8.7]
cailavikṣepāṇi cākārṣuḥ | [LalVis, 8 8.8]
sarvaṃ ca kapilavastumahānagaraṃ ṣaḍvikāraṃ prākampitam | [LalVis, 8 8.9]
divyāni ca kusumāni prāvarṣan | [LalVis, 8 8.10]
tūryaśatasahasrāṇi cāghaṭṭitāni praṇeduḥ | [LalVis, 8 8.11]
yeṣāṃ ca devānāṃ tāḥ pratimās te sarve svasvarūpamupadarśyemā gāthā abhāṣata | [LalVis, 8 8.12]
asmin khalu punarbhikṣavo bodhisattvena mahāsattvena devakule praveśe saṃdarśyamāne dvātriṃśatāṃ devaputraśatasahasrāṇāmanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittānyutpadyante | [LalVis, 8 11.1]
ayaṃ bhikṣavo heturayaṃ pratyayo yenopekṣako bodhisattvo bhavati sma devakulamupanīyamāna iti | [LalVis, 8 11.2]
{LalVis, 9}
atha khalu bhikṣava udayano nāma brāhmaṇo rājñaḥ purohita udāyinaḥ pitā sa pañcamātrairbrāhmaṇaśataiḥ parivṛto hastottare citrānakṣatre rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramyaivamāha yatkhalu devo jānīyādābharaṇāni kumārāya kriyantāmiti | [LalVis, 9 1.1]
taṃ rājā āha bāḍham | [LalVis, 9 1.2]
gāḍhaṃ kriyatāmiti | [LalVis, 9 1.3]
tatra rājñā śuddhodanena pañcamātraiśca śākyaśataiḥ pañcamātrāṇyābharaṇaśatāni kāritānyabhūvan | [LalVis, 9 2.1]
tadyathā hastābharaṇāni pādābharaṇāni mūrdhābharaṇāni kaṇṭhābharaṇāni mudrikābharaṇāni karṇikāyākeyūrāṇi mekhalāsuvarṇasūtrāṇi kiṅkiṇījālāni ratnajālāni maṇipratyuptāni pādukā nānāratnasamalaṃkṛtā hārāḥ kaṭakā harṣā mukuṭāni | [LalVis, 9 2.2]
kārayitvā ca puṣyanakṣatrayogenānuyuktena te śākyā rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramyaivamāhur hanta deva maṇḍyatāṃ kumāra iti | [LalVis, 9 2.3]
rājā āha alamalaṃkṛtaśca pūjitaśca bhavadbhiḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 9 2.4]
mayāpi kumārasya sarvābharaṇāni kāritāni | [LalVis, 9 2.5]
te 'vocan saptasaptarātriṃdivānyapyasmākamābharaṇāni kumāraḥ kāya ābadhnātu | [LalVis, 9 2.6]
tato 'smākamamogho vyāyāmo bhaviṣyatīti | [LalVis, 9 2.7]
tatra rātrau vinirgatāyāmāditya udite vimalavyūhanāmodyānaṃ tatra bodhisattvo nirgato 'bhūt | [LalVis, 9 3.1]
tatra mahāprajāpatyā gautamyā bodhisattvo 'ṅke gṛhīto 'bhūt | [LalVis, 9 3.2]
aśītiśca strīsahasrāṇi pratyudgamya bodhisattvasya vadanaṃ prekṣante sma | [LalVis, 9 3.3]
daśa ca kanyāsahasrāṇi pratyudgamya bodhisattvasya vadanaṃ prekṣante sma | [LalVis, 9 3.4]
pañca ca brāhmaṇasahasrāṇi pratyudgamya bodhisattvasya vadanaṃ prekṣante sma | [LalVis, 9 3.5]
tatra yāni bhadrikeṇa śākyarājenābharaṇāni kāritānyabhūvan tāni bodhisattvasya kāye ābadhyante sma | [LalVis, 9 3.6]
tāni samanantarābaddhāni bodhisattvasya kāyaprabhayā jihmīkṛtānyabhūvan na bhāsante sma na tapanti sma na virocanti sma | [LalVis, 9 3.7]
tadyathāpi nāma jāmbūnadasya suvarṇasya purato masipiṇḍa upanikṣipto na bhāsati na tapati na virocate evameva tānyābharaṇāni bodhisattvasya kāyaprabhayā spṛṣṭāni na bhāsante na tapanti na virocante sma | [LalVis, 9 3.8]
evaṃ yā yā ābharaṇavikṛtirbodhisattvasya kāya ābadhyate sma sā sā jihmībhavati sma tadyathāpi nāma masipiṇḍaḥ | [LalVis, 9 3.9]
tatra vimalā nāmodyānadevatā sā audārikam ātmabhāvam abhisaṃdarśya purataḥ sthitvā rājānaṃ śuddhodanaṃ taṃ ca mahāntaṃ śākyagaṇaṃ gāthābhirabhibhāṣate sma | [LalVis, 9 4.1]
ityuktvā sā devatā bodhisattvaṃ divyaiḥ puṣpairabhyavakīrya tatraivāntaradhāt | [LalVis, 9 10.1]
{LalVis, 10}
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ saṃvṛddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 10 1.1]
tadā māṅgalyaśatasahasraiḥ lipiśālām upanīyate sma daśabhirdārakasahasraiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛtaḥ daśabhiśca rathasahasraiḥ khādanīyabhojanīyasvādanīyaparipūrṇair hiraṇyasuvarṇaparipūrṇaiśca | [LalVis, 10 1.2]
yena kapilavastuni mahānagare vīthicatvararathyāntarāpaṇamukheṣv abhyavakīryate sma abhiviśrāmyante | [LalVis, 10 1.3]
aṣṭābhiśca tūryaśatasahasraiḥ praghuṣyamāṇairmahatā ca puṣpavarṣeṇābhipravarṣatā vitardiniryūhatoraṇagavākṣaharmyakūṭāgāraprāsādataleṣu kanyāśatasahasrāṇi sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ sthitā abhūvan | [LalVis, 10 1.4]
bodhisattvaṃ prekṣamāṇāḥ kusumāni ca kṣipanti sma | [LalVis, 10 1.5]

taṃ tathā prapatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śubhāṅgo nāma tuṣitakāyiko devaputro dakṣiṇena karatalena parigṛhyotthāpayati sma | [LalVis, 10 2.3]

{LalVis, 12}
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ saṃvṛddhe kumāre rājā śuddhodano 'pareṇa samayena śākyagaṇena sārdhaṃ saṃsthāgāre niṣaṇṇo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 1.2]
tatra te mahallakamahallakāḥ śākyā rājānaṃ śuddhodanamevamāhuḥ yatkhalu devo jānīyāt | [LalVis, 12 1.3]
ayaṃ sarvārthasiddhakumāro naimittikairbrāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaniścayaiśca devairyadbhūyasaivaṃ nirdiṣṭo yadi kumāro 'bhiniṣkramiṣyati tathāgato bhaviṣyatyarhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [LalVis, 12 1.4]
uta nābhiniṣkramiṣyati rājā bhaviṣyati cakravartī caturaṅgo vijitavān dhārmiko dharmarājaḥ saptaratnasamanvāgataḥ | [LalVis, 12 1.5]
tasyemāni sapta ratnāni bhaviṣyanti | [LalVis, 12 1.6]
tadyathā cakraratnaṃ hastiratnaṃ aśvaratnaṃ maṇiratnaṃ strīratnaṃ gṛhapatiratnaṃ pariṇāyakaratnam | [LalVis, 12 1.7]
evaṃ saptaratnam | [LalVis, 12 1.8]
sampūrṇaṃ cāsya putrasahasraṃ bhaviṣyati śūrāṇāṃ varāṅgarūpiṇāṃ parasainyapramardakānām | [LalVis, 12 1.9]
sa imaṃ pṛthivīmaṇḍalamadaṇḍenāśastreṇābhinirjityādhyāvasiṣyati saha dharmeṇeti | [LalVis, 12 1.10]
tasmānniveśanaṃ kumārasya kriyatāmiti | [LalVis, 12 1.11]
tatra strīgaṇaparivṛto ratiṃ vetsyati nābhiniṣkramiṣyati | [LalVis, 12 1.12]
evamasmākaṃ cakravartivaṃśasya cānupacchedo bhaviṣyati | [LalVis, 12 1.13]
mānitāśca bhaviṣyāmo 'navadyāśca sarvakoṭarājabhiḥ | [LalVis, 12 1.14]
tato rājā śuddhodana evamāha yadyevaṃ tena hi vyavalokayata katamā kanyā kumārasyānurūpā syāt | [LalVis, 12 2.1]
tatra pañcamātrāṇi śākyaśatāni | [LalVis, 12 2.2]
ekaika evamāha mama duhitā anurūpā syāt kumārasya | [LalVis, 12 2.3]
surūpā mama duhiteti | [LalVis, 12 2.4]
rājā prāha durāsadaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 12 2.5]
tat prativedayiṣyāmastāvat kumārasya katamā te kanyā rocata iti | [LalVis, 12 2.6]
tataśca te sarve saṃnipatya kumārasyaināṃ prakṛtimārocayanti sma | [LalVis, 12 2.7]
tān kumāra uvāca saptame divase prativacanaṃ śroṣyatheti | [LalVis, 12 2.8]
sa punarapi mīmāṃsopāyakauśalyam āmukhīkṛtya sattvaparipākamavekṣamāṇo mahākaruṇāṃ saṃjanayya tasyāṃ velāyāmimāṃ gāthāmabhāṣata | [LalVis, 12 6.1]
atha khalu bhikṣavo rājā śuddhodana imā gāthā vācayitvā purohitamāmantrayate sma gaccha tvaṃ mahābrāhmaṇa kapilavastumahānagare | [LalVis, 12 17.1]
sarvagṛhāṇyanupraviśya kanyā vyavalokaya | [LalVis, 12 17.2]
yasyā ete guṇāḥ saṃvidyante kṣatriyakanyāyā vā brāhmaṇakanyāyā vā vaiśyakanyāyā vā śūdrakanyāyā vā tāṃ kanyāmasmākaṃ prativedaya | [LalVis, 12 17.3]
tatkasmāddhetor na hi kumāraḥ kulārthiko na gotrārthikaḥ | [LalVis, 12 17.4]
guṇārthika eva kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 12 17.5]
tasyāṃ ca velāyāmimāṃ gāthāmabhāṣata | [LalVis, 12 18.1]
brāhmaṇīṃ kṣatriyāṃ kanyāṃ veśyāṃ śūdrīṃ tathaiva ca | [LalVis, 12 19.1]
yasyā ete guṇāḥ santi tāṃ me kanyāṃ pravedaya | [LalVis, 12 19.2]
na kulena na gotreṇa kumāro mama vismitaḥ | [LalVis, 12 20.1]
guṇe satye ca dharme ca tatrāsya ramate manaḥ | [LalVis, 12 20.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavaḥ sa purohitastaṃ gāthālekhaṃ gṛhītvā kapilavastuni mahānagare gṛhādgṛhaṃ vyavalokayan gatvā hiṇḍan kanyāṃ paryeṣate sma | [LalVis, 12 21.1]
evaṃguṇayuktām apaśyan na caiva guṇayuktāṃ kanyāṃ | [LalVis, 12 21.2]
so 'nupūrveṇa vicaran yena daṇḍapāṇeḥ śākyasya niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 12 21.3]
sa taṃ niveśanaṃ praviṣṭo 'drākṣīt kanyāmabhirūpāṃ prāsādikāṃ darśanīyāṃ paramayā śubhavarṇapuṣkaratayā samanvāgatāṃ nātidīrghāṃ nātihrasvāṃ nātisthūlāṃ nātikṛśāṃ nātigaurāṃ nātikṛṣṇāṃ prathamayauvanāvasthāṃ strīratnamiva khyāyamānām | [LalVis, 12 21.4]
atha sā dārikā purohitasya caraṇau gṛhītvā evamāha kena te mahābrāhmaṇa kāryam | [LalVis, 12 21.5]
purohita āha | [LalVis, 12 21.6]
śuddhodanasya tanayaḥ paramābhirūpo dvātriṃśalakṣaṇadharo guṇatejayuktaḥ | [LalVis, 12 22.1]
teneti gātha likhitā guṇaye vadhūnāṃ yasyā guṇāsti hi ime sa hi tasya patnī | [LalVis, 12 22.2]
sa tasyāstaṃ lekhamupanāmayati sma | [LalVis, 12 23.1]
atha sā dārikā taṃ gāthālekhaṃ vācayitvā smitamupadarśya taṃ purohitaṃ gāthayādhyabhāṣat | [LalVis, 12 24.1]
mahyeti brāhmaṇa guṇā anurūpa sarve so me patirbhavatu saumya surūparūpaḥ | [LalVis, 12 25.1]
bhaṇahi kumāru yadi kārya ma hū vilamba mā hīnaprākṛtajanena bhaveya vāsaḥ | [LalVis, 12 25.2]
iti | [LalVis, 12 26.1]
atha sa khalu purohito rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramyaiva tamarthamārocayati sma dṛṣṭā mayā deva kanyā yā kumārasyānurūpā syāt | [LalVis, 12 27.1]
āha kasyāsau āha daṇḍapāṇerdeva śākyasya duhitā | [LalVis, 12 27.2]
atha rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyaitadabhavad durāsadaḥ kumāraḥ śubhādhimuktaśca | [LalVis, 12 28.1]
prāyeṇa ca mātṛgrāmo 'saṃvidyamānaguṇo 'pi guṇānāmātmani prajānīte | [LalVis, 12 28.2]
yannvahamaśokabhāṇḍakāni kārayeyam yāni kumāraḥ sarvadārikābhyo 'nuprayacchet | [LalVis, 12 28.3]
tatra yasyāṃ dārikāyāṃ kumārasya cakṣur abhiniveśyati tāṃ kumārasya varayiṣyāmīti | [LalVis, 12 28.4]
atha khalu rājā śuddhodano 'śokabhāṇḍāni kārayati sma suvarṇamayāni rūpyamayāni nānāratnamayāni | [LalVis, 12 29.1]
kārayitvā ca kapilavastuni mahānagare ghaṇṭāghoṣaṇāṃ kārayāmāsa saptame divase kumāro darśanaṃ dāsyati aśokabhāṇḍakāni ca dārikābhyo viśrāṇayiṣyati | [LalVis, 12 29.2]
tatra sarvadārikābhiḥ saṃsthāgāre saṃnipatitavyamiti | [LalVis, 12 29.3]
iti hi bhikṣavaḥ saptame divase bodhisattvaḥ saṃsthāgāramupasaṃkramya bhadrāsane nyaṣīdat | [LalVis, 12 30.1]
rājāpi śuddhodano 'dṛśyapuruṣān sthāpayati sma yasyāṃ dārikāyāṃ kumārasya cakṣuḥ saṃniviśet tāṃ mamārocayadhvamiti | [LalVis, 12 30.2]
iti hi bhikṣavo yāvantyaḥ kapilavastuni mahānagare dārikāstāḥ sarvā yena saṃsthāgāro yena ca bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāman bodhisattvasya darśanāya aśokabhāṇḍakāni ca pratigṛhītum | [LalVis, 12 31.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo yathāgatābhyastābhyo dārikābhyo 'śokabhāṇḍakānyanuprayacchati sma | [LalVis, 12 32.1]
tāśca dārikā na śaknuvanti sma bodhisattvasya śriyaṃ tejaśca soḍhum | [LalVis, 12 32.2]
tā aśokabhāṇḍakāni gṛhītvā śīghraṃ śīghrameva prakrāmanti sma | [LalVis, 12 32.3]
atha daṇḍapāṇeḥ śākyasya duhitā gopā nāma śākyakanyā sā dāsīgaṇaparivṛtā puraskṛtā yena saṃsthāgāro yena ca bodhisattvastenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 12 33.1]
upasaṃkramyaikānte 'sthāt bodhisattvamanimeṣābhyāṃ nayanābhyāṃ prekṣamāṇā | [LalVis, 12 33.2]
tadyadā bodhisattvena sarvāṇyaśokabhāṇḍāni dattāni tadā sā bodhisattvamupasaṃkramya prahasitavadanā bodhisattvamevamāha kumāra kiṃ te mayāpanītaṃ yastvaṃ māṃ vimānayasi | [LalVis, 12 33.3]
āha nāhaṃ tvāṃ vimānayāmi api tu khalu punastvamabhipaścādāgateti | [LalVis, 12 33.4]
sa tasyai cānekaśatasahasramūlyamaṅgulīyakaṃ nirmucya prādāt | [LalVis, 12 33.5]
sā prāha idamahaṃ kumāra tavāntikādarhāmi āha imāni madīyānyābharaṇāni gṛhyatām | [LalVis, 12 34.1]
sā āha na vayaṃ kumāraṃ vyalaṃkariṣyāmaḥ alaṃkariṣyāmo vayaṃ kumāram | [LalVis, 12 34.2]
ityuktvā sā kanyā prakrāmat | [LalVis, 12 34.3]
tatastairguhyapuruṣai rājānaṃ śuddhodanamupasaṃkramyaiṣa vṛttānto nivedito 'bhūd deva daṇḍapāṇeḥ śākyasya duhitā gopā nāma śākyakanyā tasyāṃ kumārasya cakṣurniviṣṭaṃ muhūrtaṃ ca tayoḥ saṃlāpo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 35.1]
ityetatkhalu vacanaṃ śrutvā rājā śuddhodano daṇḍapāṇeḥ śākyasya purohitaṃ dautyena preṣayati sma yā te duhitā sā mama kumārasya pradīyatāmiti | [LalVis, 12 36.1]
daṇḍapāṇirāha ārya kumāro gṛhe sukhasaṃvṛddhaḥ | [LalVis, 12 37.1]
asmākaṃ cāyaṃ kuladharmaḥ śilpajñasya kanyā dātavyā nāśilpajñasyeti | [LalVis, 12 37.2]
kumāraśca na śilpajño nāsidhanuṣkalāpayuddhasālambhavidhijñaḥ | [LalVis, 12 37.3]
tatkatham aśilpajñāyāhaṃ duhitaraṃ dāsyāmi | [LalVis, 12 37.4]
ityetacca rājñaḥ prativeditam | [LalVis, 12 37.5]
tato rājña etadabhavad dvirapīdamahaṃ sahadharmeṇa coditaḥ | [LalVis, 12 37.6]
yadāpi mayoktaṃ kasmācchākyakumārāḥ kumārasyopasthānāya nāgacchantīti tadāpyahamabhihitaḥ kiṃ vayaṃ maṇḍakasyopasthānaṃ kariṣyāma iti | [LalVis, 12 37.7]
etarhyapyevamiti pradhyāyanniṣaṇṇo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 37.8]
bodhisattvaścainaṃ vṛttāntamaśrauṣīt | [LalVis, 12 38.1]
śrutvā ca yena rājā śuddhodanastenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 12 38.2]
upasaṃkramyaivamāha deva kimidaṃ dīnamanāstiṣṭhasi | [LalVis, 12 38.3]
rājā āha alaṃ te kumāra anena | [LalVis, 12 38.4]
kumāra āha deva sarvathā tāvadavaśyam evamākhyātavyam | [LalVis, 12 38.5]
yāvattrirapi bodhisattvo rājānaṃ śuddhodanaṃ paripṛcchati sma | [LalVis, 12 38.6]
tato rājā śuddhodano bodhisattvāya tāṃ prakṛtimārocayati sma | [LalVis, 12 39.1]
tāṃ śrutvā bodhisattva āha deva asti punariha nagare kaścidyo mayā sārdhaṃ samarthaḥ śilpena śilpamupadarśayitum | [LalVis, 12 39.2]
tato rājā śuddhodanaḥ prahasitavadano bodhisattvamevamāha śakyasi punastvaṃ putra śilpamupadarśayitum sa āha bāḍhaṃ śakyāmi deva | [LalVis, 12 39.3]
tena hi saṃnipātyantāṃ sarvaśilpajñā yeṣāṃ purataḥ svaṃ śilpamupadarśayiṣyāmi | [LalVis, 12 39.4]
tato rājā śuddhodanaḥ kapilavastuni mahānagaravare ghaṇṭāghoṣaṇāṃ kārayati sma saptame divase kumāraḥ svaṃ śilpamupadarśayati | [LalVis, 12 40.1]
tatra sarvaśilpajñaiḥ saṃnipatitavyam | [LalVis, 12 40.2]
tatra saptame divase pañcamātrāṇi śākyakumāraśatāni saṃnipatitānyabhūvan | [LalVis, 12 41.1]
daṇḍapāṇeśca śākyasya duhitā gopā nāma śākyakanyā jayapatākā sthāpitābhūd yo vā atra asidhanuṣkalāpayuddhasālambheṣu jeṣyati tasyaiṣā bhaviṣyatīti | [LalVis, 12 41.2]
tatra sarvapurato devadattaḥ kumāro nagarādabhiniṣkrāmati sma | [LalVis, 12 42.1]
śvetaśca hastī mahāpramāṇo bodhisattvasyārthe nagaraṃ praveśyate sma | [LalVis, 12 42.2]
tatra devadattaḥ kumāra īrṣyayā ca śākyabalamadena ca mattaḥ | [LalVis, 12 42.3]
sa taṃ hastināgaṃ vāmena pāṇinā śuṇḍāyāṃ gṛhītvā dakṣiṇena pāṇinā capeṭayā ekaprahāreṇaiva hato 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 42.4]
tasyānantaraṃ sundaranandakumāro 'bhiniṣkrāmati sma | [LalVis, 12 43.1]
so 'drākṣīttaṃ hastināgaṃ nagaradvāre hatam | [LalVis, 12 43.2]
dṛṣṭvā ca paryapṛcchat kenāyaṃ hata iti | [LalVis, 12 43.3]
tatra mahājanakāya āha devadatteneti | [LalVis, 12 43.4]
sa āha aśobhanamidaṃ devadattasya | [LalVis, 12 43.5]
sa taṃ hastināgaṃ lāṅgūle gṛhītvā nagaradvārādapakarṣati sma | [LalVis, 12 43.6]
tadanantaraṃ bodhisattvo rathābhirūḍho 'bhiniṣkrāmati sma | [LalVis, 12 44.1]
adrākṣīdbodhisattvastaṃ hastinaṃ hatam | [LalVis, 12 44.2]
dṛṣṭvā ca paryapṛcchat kenāyaṃ hata iti | [LalVis, 12 44.3]
āhur devadatteneti | [LalVis, 12 44.4]
āha aśobhanaṃ devadattasya | [LalVis, 12 44.5]
kena punarasmānnagaradvārādapakarṣita iti | [LalVis, 12 44.6]
āhuḥ sundaranandeneti | [LalVis, 12 44.7]
āha śobhanamidaṃ sundaranandasya | [LalVis, 12 44.8]
kiṃtu mahākāyo 'yaṃ sattvaḥ | [LalVis, 12 44.9]
so 'yaṃ klinnaḥ sarvanagaraṃ daurgandhena sphuriṣyatīti | [LalVis, 12 44.10]
tataḥ kumāro rathasya evaikaṃ pādaṃ bhūmau prasārya pādāṅguṣṭhena taṃ hastināgaṃ lāṅgūle gṛhītvā sapta prākārān sapta ca parikhānatikramya bahirnagarasya krośamātre prakṣipati sma | [LalVis, 12 45.1]
yatra ca pradeśe sa hastī patitastasmin pradeśe mahadbilaṃ saṃvṛttaṃ yatsāṃprataṃ hastigartetyabhidhīyate | [LalVis, 12 45.2]
tatra devamanujāḥ śatasahasrāṇi hāhākārakilakilāprakṣveḍitaśatasahasrāṇi prāmuñcan | [LalVis, 12 46.1]
cailavikṣepāṃścākārṣuḥ | [LalVis, 12 46.2]
gaganatalagatāśca devaputrā ime gāthe 'bhāṣanta | [LalVis, 12 46.3]
iti hi pañcamātrāṇi śākyakumāraśatāni nagarānniṣkramya yenānyatamaḥ pṛthivīpradeśo yatra śākyakumārāḥ śilpamupadarśayanti sma tenopasaṃkrāman | [LalVis, 12 49.1]
rājāpi śuddhodano mahallakamahallakāśca śākyā mahāṃśca janakāyo yenāsau pṛthivīpradeśastenopasaṃkrāman bodhisattvasya cānyeṣāṃ ca śākyakumārāṇāṃ śilpaviśeṣaṃ draṣṭukāmāḥ | [LalVis, 12 49.2]
tatra ādita eva ye śākyakumārā lipyāṃ paṭuvidhijñāste bodhisattvena sārdhaṃ lipiṃ viśeṣayanti sma | [LalVis, 12 50.1]
tatra taiḥ śākyairviśvāmitra ācāryaḥ sākṣī sthāpito 'bhūt sa tvaṃ vyavalokaya katamo 'tra kumāro lipijñāne viśiṣyate yadi vā lekhyato yadi vā bahulipiniryāṇataḥ | [LalVis, 12 50.2]
atha viśvāmitra ācāryaḥ pratyakṣo bodhisattvasya lipijñāne smitamupadarśayannime gāthe 'bhāṣata | [LalVis, 12 50.3]
śākyā āhur viśiṣyatāṃ tāvatkumāro lipijñāne | [LalVis, 12 53.1]
saṃkhyājñāne kumāro viśeṣayitavyo jijñāsyaśca | [LalVis, 12 53.2]
tatrārjuno nāma śākyagaṇako mahāmātraḥ saṃkhyāgaṇanāsu pāraṃgataḥ sa sākṣī sthāpito 'bhūt sa tvaṃ vyavalokaya katamo 'tra kumāro viśiṣyate saṃkhyājñānata iti | [LalVis, 12 53.3]
tatra bodhisattvaścoddiśati sma ekaśca śākyakumāro nikṣipati sma na ca pariprāpayati sma | [LalVis, 12 53.4]
bodhisattvasyaiko dvau trayaścatvāraḥ pañcadaśa viṃśattriṃśaccatvāriṃśatpañcāśacchataṃ yāvatpañcāpi śākyakumāraśatāni yugapatkāle nikṣipanti sma na ca pariprāpayanti sma | [LalVis, 12 53.5]
tato bodhisattva āha uddiśata yūyam ahaṃ nikṣepsyāmīti | [LalVis, 12 53.6]
tatraikaśākyakumāro bodhisattvasyoddiśati sma na ca pariprāpayati sma | [LalVis, 12 53.7]
dvāvapi trayo 'pi pañcāpi daśāpi viṃśatyapi triṃśadapi catvāriṃśadapi pañcāśadapi yāvatpañcāpi śākyakumāraśatāni yugapaduddiśanti sma | [LalVis, 12 53.8]
na ca pariprāpayanti sma bodhisattvasya nikṣipataḥ | [LalVis, 12 53.9]
bodhisattva āha alamalamanena vivādena | [LalVis, 12 54.1]
sarva idānīmekībhūtvā mamoddiśata ahaṃ nikṣepsyāmīti | [LalVis, 12 54.2]
tatra pañcamātrāṇi śākyakumāraśatāny ekavacanodāhāreṇāpūrvacaritaṃ samuddiśanti sma bodhisattvaścāsaṃmūḍho nikṣipati sma | [LalVis, 12 54.3]
evamaparyantāḥ sarvaśākyakumārāḥ atha paryantaśca bodhisattvaḥ | [LalVis, 12 54.4]
tato 'rjuno gaṇakamahāmātra āścaryaprāpta ime gāthe 'bhāṣata | [LalVis, 12 55.1]
tataḥ sarvaśākyagaṇa āścaryaprāptaḥ paramavismayāpanno 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 58.1]
ekakaṇṭhāścemāṃ vācamabhāṣanta jayati jayati bhoḥ sarvārthasiddhaḥ kumāraḥ | [LalVis, 12 58.2]
sarve cāsanebhya utthāya kṛtāñjalipuṭā bhūtvā bodhisattvaṃ namaskṛtya rājānaṃ śuddhodanametadavocan lābhāste mahārāja paramasulabdhāḥ yasya te putra evaṃ śīghralaghujavacapalaparipṛcchāpratibhāna iti | [LalVis, 12 58.3]
atha sa rājā śuddhodano bodhisattvamevamāha śakyasi putra arjunena gaṇakamahāmātreṇa sārdhaṃ saṃkhyājñānakauśalyagaṇanāgatim anupraveṣṭuṃ tena hi gaṇyatām | [LalVis, 12 59.1]
athārjuno gaṇakamahāmātro bodhisattvamevamāha jānīṣe tvaṃ kumāra koṭiśatottarāṃ nāma gaṇanāgatiṃ bodhisattva āha śakyāmi deva | [LalVis, 12 59.2]
āha jānāmyaham | [LalVis, 12 59.3]
āha kathaṃ punaḥ koṭiśatottarā gaṇanāgatiranupraveṣṭavyā bodhisattva āha śataṃ koṭīnāmayutaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.4]
śatamayutānāṃ niyuto nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.5]
śataṃ niyutānāṃ kaṅkaraṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.6]
śataṃ kaṅkarāṇāṃ vivaraṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.7]
śataṃ vivarāṇām akṣobhyaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.8]
śatamakṣobhyāṇāṃ vivāhaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.9]
śataṃ vivāhānāmutsaṅgaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.10]
śatamutsaṅgānāṃ bahulaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.11]
śataṃ bahulānāṃ nāgabalaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.12]
śataṃ nāgabalānāṃ tiṭilambhaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.13]
śataṃ tiṭilambhānāṃ vyavasthānaprajñaptir nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.14]
śataṃ vyavasthānaprajñaptīnāṃ hetuhilaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.15]
śataṃ hetuhilānāṃ karakurnāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.16]
śataṃ karakūṇāṃ hetvindriyaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.17]
śataṃ hetvindriyāṇāṃ samāptalambhaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.18]
śataṃ samāptalambhānāṃ gaṇanāgatirnāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.19]
śataṃ gaṇanāgatīnāṃ niravadyaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.20]
śataṃ niravadyānāṃ mudrābalaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.21]
śataṃ mudrābalānāṃ sarvabalaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.22]
śataṃ sarvabalānāṃ visaṃjñāgatī nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.23]
śataṃ visaṃjñāgatīnāṃ sarvasaṃjñā nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.24]
śataṃ sarvasaṃjñānāṃ vibhūtaṃgamā nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.25]
śataṃ vibhūtaṃgamānāṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ nāmocyate | [LalVis, 12 59.26]
iti hi tallakṣaṇagaṇanayā sumeruparvatarājo lakṣanikṣepakriyayā parikṣayaṃ gacchet | [LalVis, 12 59.27]
ato 'pyuttari dhvajāgravatī nāma gaṇanā yasyāṃ gaṇanāyāṃ gaṅgānadīvālikāsamā lakṣanikṣepakriyayā parikṣayaṃ gaccheyuḥ | [LalVis, 12 59.28]
ato 'pyuttari dhvajāgraniśāmaṇī nāma gaṇanā | [LalVis, 12 59.29]
ato 'pyuttari vāhanaprajñaptirnāma | [LalVis, 12 59.30]
ato 'pyuttari iṅgā nāma | [LalVis, 12 59.31]
ato 'pyuttari kuruṭu nāma | [LalVis, 12 59.32]
ato 'pyuttari kuruṭāvi nāma | [LalVis, 12 59.33]
ato 'pyuttari sarvanikṣepā nāma gaṇanā yasyāṃ gaṇanāyāṃ daśa gaṅgānadīvālikāsamā lakṣanikṣepakriyayā parikṣayaṃ gaccheyuḥ | [LalVis, 12 59.34]
ato 'pyuttari agrasārā nāma gaṇanā yatra koṭīśataṃ gaṅgānadīvālikāsamā lakṣanikṣepāḥ parikṣayaṃ gaccheyuḥ | [LalVis, 12 59.35]
ato 'pyuttari paramāṇurajaḥpraveśānugatānāṃ gaṇanā yatra tathāgataṃ sthāpayitvā bodhimaṇḍavarāgragataṃ ca sarvadharmābhiṣekābhimukhaṃ bodhisattvaṃ nānyaḥ kaścitsattvaḥ sattvanikāye saṃvidyate ya etāṃ gaṇanāṃ prajānāti anyatrāhaṃ vā yo vā syānmādṛśaḥ | [LalVis, 12 59.36]
evaṃ caramabhāviko viniṣkrāntagṛhavāso bodhisattvaḥ | [LalVis, 12 59.37]
arjuno 'vocat kathaṃ kumāra paramāṇurajaḥpraveśagaṇanānupraveṣṭavyā bodhisattva āha sapta paramāṇurajāṃsyaṇuḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.1]
saptāṇavastrutiḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.2]
saptatruterekaṃ vātāyanarajaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.3]
sapta vātāyanarajāṃsyekaṃ śaśarajaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.4]
sapta śaśarajāṃsyekameḍakarajaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.5]
saptaiḍakarajāṃsyekaṃ gorajaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.6]
sapta gorajāṃsyekaṃ likṣārajaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.7]
sapta likṣāḥ sarṣapaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.8]
saptasarṣapādyavaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.9]
saptayavādaṅgulīparva | [LalVis, 12 60.10]
dvādaśāṅgulīparvāṇi vitastiḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.11]
dve vitastī hastaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.12]
catvāro hastā dhanuḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.13]
dhanuḥsahasraṃ mārgadhvajākrośaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.14]
catvāraḥ krośā yojanam | [LalVis, 12 60.15]
tatra ko yuṣmākaṃ yojanapiṇḍaṃ prajānāti kiyanti tāni paramāṇurajāṃsi bhavanti arjuno 'vocad ahameva tāvatkumāra saṃmohamāpannaḥ kimaṅga punarye cānye 'lpabuddhayaḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.16]
nirdiśatu kumāro yojanapiṇḍaṃ kiyanti tāni paramāṇurajāṃsi bhavantīti | [LalVis, 12 60.17]
bodhisattvo 'vocat tatra yojanapiṇḍaḥ paramāṇurajasāṃ paripūrṇamakṣobhyanayutamekaṃ triṃśacca koṭīnayutaśatasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiśca koṭīśatāni dvātriṃśatiśca koṭyaḥ pañca ca daśaśatasahasrāṇi dvādaśa ca sahasrāṇi etāvān yojanapiṇḍaḥ paramāṇurajonikṣepasya | [LalVis, 12 60.18]
anena praveśenāyaṃ jambudvīpaḥ saptayojanasahasrāṇi | [LalVis, 12 60.19]
godānīyo 'ṣṭau yojanasahasrāṇi | [LalVis, 12 60.20]
pūrvavideho nava yojanasahasrāṇi | [LalVis, 12 60.21]
uttarakurudvīpo daśayojanasahasrāṇi | [LalVis, 12 60.22]
anena praveśenemaṃ cāturdvīpakaṃ lokadhātuṃ pramukhaṃ kṛtvā paripūrṇakoṭīśataṃ cāturdvīpakānāṃ lokadhātūnāṃ yatra koṭīśataṃ mahāsamudrāṇām koṭīśataṃ cakravālamahācakravālānām koṭīśataṃ sumerūṇāṃ parvatarajānām koṭīśataṃ caturmahārājikānāṃ devānām koṭīśataṃ trayastriṃśānām koṭīśataṃ yāmānām koṭīśataṃ tuṣitānām koṭīśataṃ nirmāṇaratīnām koṭīśataṃ paranirmitavaśavartīnām koṭīśataṃ brahmakāyikānām koṭīśataṃ brahmapurohitānām koṭīśataṃ brahmapārṣadyānām koṭīśataṃ mahābrahmāṇām koṭīśataṃ parīttābhānām koṭīśataṃ apramāṇābhānām koṭīśataṃ ābhāsvarāṇām koṭīśataṃ parīttaśubhānām koṭīśataṃ apramāṇaśubhānām koṭīśataṃ śubhakṛtsnānām koṭīśataṃ anabhrakāṇām koṭīśataṃ puṇyaprasavānām koṭīśataṃ bṛhatphalānām koṭīśataṃ asaṃjñisattvānām koṭīśataṃ abṛhānām koṭīśataṃ atapānām koṭīśataṃ sudṛśānām koṭīśataṃ sudarśanānām koṭīśataṃ akaniṣṭhānāṃ devānām | [LalVis, 12 60.23]
ayamucyate trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhāturvipulaśca vistīrṇaśca | [LalVis, 12 60.24]
sa yāvanti yojanaśatāni paramāṇurajāṃsi trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātau yāvanti yojanasahasrāṇi yāvanti yojanakoṭayaḥ yāvanti yojananayutāni ........ peyālaṃ ............. yāvadyāvanto yojanāgrasārā gaṇanāḥ | [LalVis, 12 60.25]
kiyantyetāni paramāṇurajāṃsi ityāha | [LalVis, 12 60.26]
saṃkhyāgaṇanā vyativṛttā hyeṣāṃ gaṇanānāṃ taducyate 'saṃkhyeyamiti | [LalVis, 12 60.27]
ato 'saṃkhyeyatamāni paramāṇurajāṃsi yāni trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātau bhavanti | [LalVis, 12 60.28]
asmin khalu punargaṇanāparivarte bodhisattvena nirdiśyamāne arjuno gaṇakamahāmātraḥ sarvaśca śākyagaṇastuṣṭa udagra āttamanāḥ pramudita āścaryādbhutaprāpto 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 61.1]
te sarva ekaikairvastraiḥ sthitā abhūvan | [LalVis, 12 61.2]
pariśiṣṭairvastrābharaṇairbodhisattvam abhicchādayanti sma | [LalVis, 12 61.3]
atha khalvarjuno gaṇakamahāmātra ime gāthe 'bhāṣata | [LalVis, 12 62.1]
tatra devamanujāḥ śatasahasrāṇi hāhākārakilikilāprakṣveḍitaśatasahasrāṇi prāmuñcan | [LalVis, 12 66.1]
gaganatalagatāśca devaputrā imā gāthā abhāṣanta | [LalVis, 12 66.2]
iti hi bhikṣavo 'bhibhūtāḥ sarve śākyakumārā abhūvan | [LalVis, 12 68.1]
bodhisattva eva viśiṣyate | [LalVis, 12 68.2]
tadanantaraṃ laṅghite plavite javite sarvatra bodhisattva eva viśiṣyate sma | [LalVis, 12 68.3]
gaganatalagatāśca devaputrā imāṃ gāthāmabhāṣanta | [LalVis, 12 68.4]
vratatapasaguṇena saṃyamena kṣamadamamaitrabalena kalpakoṭyaḥ | [LalVis, 12 69.1]
atha kṛtulaghukāyacittanetā tasya javasya viśeṣatāṃ śṛṇotha | [LalVis, 12 69.2]
evaṃ kṛtvā bodhisattva eva viśiṣyate sma | [LalVis, 12 72.1]
tatra śākyā āhur yuddheṣu tāvatkumāro viśeṣayitavyo jijñāsyaśca | [LalVis, 12 73.1]
tatra bodhisattva ekānte sthito 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 73.2]
tāni ca pañcamātrāṇi śākyakumāraśatāni yugapadyudhyanti sma | [LalVis, 12 73.3]
iti hi dvātriṃśacchākyakumārāḥ sālambhāya sthitāḥ | [LalVis, 12 74.1]
tadā nandaścānandaśca bodhisattvamabhigatau sālambhāya | [LalVis, 12 74.2]
tau samanantaraṃ spṛṣṭāveva bodhisattvena pāṇinā | [LalVis, 12 74.3]
tau bodhisattvasya balaṃ tejaścāsahamānau dharaṇītale prapatitāvabhūtām | [LalVis, 12 74.4]
tadanantaraṃ devadattaḥ kumāro garvitaśca mānī ca balavāneva tabdhaḥ śākyamānena ca tabdho bodhisattvena sārdhaṃ vispardhamānaḥ sarvāvantaṃ raṅgamaṇḍalaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya vikrīḍamāno bodhisattvamabhipatati sma | [LalVis, 12 74.5]
atha bodhisattvo 'saṃbhrānta evātvaran dakṣiṇena pāṇinā salīlaṃ devadattaṃ kumāraṃ gṛhītvā trirgaganatale parivartya mānanigrahārthamavihiṃsābuddhyā maitreṇa cittena dharaṇītale nikṣipati sma | [LalVis, 12 74.6]
na cāsya kāyaṃ vyābādhate sma | [LalVis, 12 74.7]
tato bodhisattvo 'pyāha alamalamanena vivādena | [LalVis, 12 75.1]
sarva eva ekībhūtvā idānīṃ sālambhāyāgacchateti | [LalVis, 12 75.2]
atha te sarve harṣitā bhūtvā bodhisattvamabhinipatitāḥ | [LalVis, 12 76.1]
te samanantaraspṛṣṭā bodhisattvena bodhisattvasya śriyaṃ tejaśca kāyabalaṃ sthāmaṃ cāsahamānāḥ spṛṣṭamātrā eva bodhisattvena dharaṇitale prāpatan | [LalVis, 12 76.2]
tatra marunmanujaśatasahasrāṇi hīhīkārakilakilāprakṣveḍitaśatasahasrāṇyakārṣuḥ | [LalVis, 12 76.3]
gaganatalagatāśca devaputrā mahāntaṃ puṣpavarṣamabhipravṛṣyaikasvareṇemāṃ gāthāmabhāṣanta | [LalVis, 12 76.4]
evaṃ kṛtvā bodhisattva eva viśiṣyate sma | [LalVis, 12 80.1]
atha daṇḍapāṇiḥ śākyakumārānetadavocaj jijñāsitamidaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ ca | [LalVis, 12 81.1]
hantedānīmiṣukṣepam upadarśayateti | [LalVis, 12 81.2]
tatra ānandasya dvayoḥ krośayorayasmayī bherī lakṣaṃ sthāpitābhūt | [LalVis, 12 81.3]
asyānantaraṃ devadattasya caturṣu krośeṣvayasmayī bherī sthāpitābhūt | [LalVis, 12 81.4]
daṇḍapāṇeryojanadvaye 'yasmayī bherī sthāpitābhūt | [LalVis, 12 81.5]
bodhisattvasya daśasu krośeṣvayasmayī bherī sthāpitābhūt | [LalVis, 12 81.6]
tasyānantaraṃ saptatālā ayasmayī varāhapratimā yantrayuktā sthāpitābhūt | [LalVis, 12 81.7]
tatrānandena dvābhyāṃ krośābhyāṃ bheryāhatābhūt tatottari na śaknoti sma | [LalVis, 12 81.8]
devadattena catuḥkrośasthā bheryāhatābhūt nottari śaknoti sma | [LalVis, 12 81.9]
sundaranandena ṣaṭkrośasthā bheryāhatābhūt nottari śaknoti sma | [LalVis, 12 81.10]
daṇḍapāṇinā dviyojanasthā bheryāhatābhūt nirviddhā ca nottari śaknoti sma | [LalVis, 12 81.11]
tatra bodhisattvasya yadyadeva dhanurupānamyate sma tattadeva vicchidyate sma | [LalVis, 12 81.12]
tato bodhisattva āha astīha deva nagare kiṃcidanyaddhanuryanmamāropaṇaṃ saheta kāyabalasthāmaṃ ca rājāhāsti putra | [LalVis, 12 81.13]
kumāra āha kva taddeva rājā āha tava putra pitāmahaḥ siṃhahanurnāmābhūt tasya yaddhanustadeva tarhi devakule gandhamālyairmahīyate | [LalVis, 12 81.14]
na punastatkaścicchaknoti sma taddhanurāropayituṃ prāgeva pūrayitum | [LalVis, 12 81.15]
bodhisattva āha ānīyatāṃ deva taddhanuḥ | [LalVis, 12 81.16]
jijñāsiṣyāmahe | [LalVis, 12 81.17]
tāvadyāvattaddhanur upanāmitamabhūt | [LalVis, 12 82.1]
tatra sarve śākyakumārāḥ parameṇāpi prayatnena vyāyacchamānā na śaknuvanti sma taddhanurāropayituṃ prāgeva pūrayitum | [LalVis, 12 82.2]
tatastaddhanurdaṇḍapāṇeḥ śākyasyopanāmitamabhūt | [LalVis, 12 82.3]
atha daṇḍapāṇiḥ śākyaḥ sarvaṃ kāyabalasthāma saṃjanayya taddhanurāropayitumārabdho 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 82.4]
na ca śaknoti sma | [LalVis, 12 82.5]
yāvadbodhisattvasyopanāmitamabhūt | [LalVis, 12 82.6]
tadbodhisattvo gṛhītvā āsanād anuttiṣṭhannevārdhaparyaṅkaṃ kṛtvā vāmena pāṇinā gṛhītvā dakṣiṇena pāṇinā ekāṅgulyagreṇāropitavānabhūt | [LalVis, 12 82.7]
tasya dhanuṣa āropyamāṇasya sarvaṃ kapilavastu mahānagaraṃ śabdenābhivijñaptamabhūt | [LalVis, 12 82.8]
sarvanagarajanaśca vihvalībhūto 'nyonyamapṛcchat kasyāyamevaṃvidhaḥ śabda iti | [LalVis, 12 82.9]
anye tadavocan siddhārthena kila kumāreṇa paitāmahadhanurāropitaṃ tasyāyaṃ śabda iti | [LalVis, 12 82.10]
tatra devamanujaśatasahasrāṇi hāhākārakilikilāprakṣveḍitaśatasahasrāṇi prāmuñcan | [LalVis, 12 82.11]
gaganatalagatāśca devaputrā rājānaṃ śuddhodanaṃ taṃ ca mahāntaṃ janakāyaṃ gāthayādhyabhāṣanta | [LalVis, 12 82.12]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvastaddhanuḥ pūrayitveṣuṃ gṛhītvā tādṛśena balasthāmnā tamiṣuṃ kṣipati sma yena yā cānandasya bherī yā ca devadattasya yāvatsundaranandasya yāvaddaṇḍapāṇestāḥ sarvā abhinirbhidya tāṃ ca daśakrośasthāṃ svakāmayasmayīṃ bherīṃ saptatālāṃ yantrayuktavarāhapratimāmabhinirbhidya sa iṣurdharaṇītalaṃ praviśya adarśanābhāso 'bhūt | [LalVis, 12 84.1]
yatra ca pradeśe sa iṣurbhūmitalaṃ bhittvā praviṣṭastasmin pradeśe kūpaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ yadadyatve 'pi śarakūpa ityabhidhīyate | [LalVis, 12 84.2]
tatra devamanuṣyaśatasahasrāṇi hīhīkārakilikilāprakṣveḍitaśatasahasrāṇi prāmuñcan | [LalVis, 12 84.3]
sarvaśca śākyagaṇo vismito 'bhūd āścaryaprāpta āścaryaṃ bhoḥ | [LalVis, 12 84.4]
na ca nāma anena yogyā kṛtā idaṃ cedṛśaṃ śilpakauśalam | [LalVis, 12 84.5]
gaganatalagatāśca devaputrā rājānaṃ śuddhodanaṃ taṃ ca mahāntaṃ janakāyamevamāhuḥ ko 'tra vismayo manujāḥ | [LalVis, 12 84.6]
tatkasmāt | [LalVis, 12 84.7]
eṣa dharaṇimaṇḍe pūrvabuddhāsanasthaḥ śamathadhanu gṛhītvā śūnyanairātmabāṇaiḥ | [LalVis, 12 85.1]
kleśaripu nihatvā dṛṣṭijālaṃ ca bhittvā śivavirajamaśokāṃ prāpsyate bodhimagryām | [LalVis, 12 85.2]
evamuktvā te devaputrā bodhisattvaṃ divyaiḥ puṣpairabhyavakīrya prākrāman | [LalVis, 12 86.1]
evaṃ laṅghite prāgval lipimudrāgaṇanāsaṃkhyasālambhadhanurvede javite plavite taraṇe iṣvastre hastigrīvāyāmaśvapṛṣṭhe rathe dhanuṣkalāpe sthairyasthāmni suśaurye bāhuvyāyāme aṅkuśagrahe pāśagrahe udyāne niryāṇe avayāne muṣṭibandhe padabandhe śikhābandhe chedye bhedye dālane sphālane akṣuṇṇavedhitve marmavedhitve śabdavedhitve dṛḍhaprahāritve akṣakrīḍāyāṃ kāvyakaraṇe granthe citre rūpe rūpakarmaṇi dhīte agnikarmaṇi vīṇāyāṃ vādye nṛtye gīte paṭhite ākhyāne hāsye lāsye nāṭye viḍambite mālyagrathane saṃvāhite maṇirāge vastrarāge māyākṛte svapnādhyāye śakunirute strīlakṣaṇe puruṣalakṣaṇe aśvalakṣaṇe hastilakṣaṇe golakṣaṇe ajalakṣaṇe miśralakṣaṇe kauṭubheśvaralakṣaṇe nirghaṇṭe nigame purāṇe itihāse vede vyākaraṇe nirukte śikṣāyāṃ chandasvinyāṃ yajñakalpe jyotiṣe sāṃkhye yoge kriyākalpe vaiśike vaiśeṣike arthavidyāyāṃ bārhaspatye āmbhirye āsurye mṛgapakṣirute hetuvidyāyāṃ jalayantre madhūcchiṣṭakṛte sūcikarmaṇi vidalakarmaṇi patrachede gandhayuktau ityevamādyāsu sarvakarmakalāsu laukikādiṣu divyamānuṣyakātikrāntāsu sarvatra bodhisattva eva viśiṣyate sma | [LalVis, 12 87.1]
atha khalu punastena samayena daṇḍapāṇiḥ śākyaḥ svāṃ duhitaraṃ gopāṃ śākyakanyāṃ bodhisattvāya prādāt | [LalVis, 12 88.1]
sā ca rājñā śuddhodanenānupūrveṇa bodhisattvasya vṛtābhūt | [LalVis, 12 88.2]
tatra khalvapi bodhisattvaś caturaśītistrīsahasrāṇāṃ madhye prāpto lokānubhavanatayā ramamāṇaṃ krīḍayantaṃ paricārayantamātmānamupadarśayati sma | [LalVis, 12 89.1]
tāsāṃ caturaśīteḥ strīsahasrāṇāṃ gopā śākyakanyā sarvāsāmagramahiṣyabhiṣiktābhūt | [LalVis, 12 89.2]
tatra khalvapi gopā śākyakanyā na kaṃcid dṛṣṭvā vadanaṃ chādayati sma śvaśrūṃ vā śvaśuraṃ vāntarjanaṃ vā | [LalVis, 12 90.1]
te tāmupadhyāyanti sma vicārayanti sma navavadhūkā hi nāma pratilīnā tiṣṭhati iyaṃ punarvivṛtaiva sarvadā iti | [LalVis, 12 90.2]
tato gopā śākyakanyā etāṃ prakṛtiṃ śrutvā sarvasyāntarjanasya purataḥ sthitvā imā gāthā abhāṣata | [LalVis, 12 90.3]
vivṛtaḥ śobhate ārya āsanasthānacaṃkrame | [LalVis, 12 91.1]
maṇiratnaṃ dhvajāgre vā bhāsamānaṃ prabhāsvaram | [LalVis, 12 91.2]
gacchan vai śobhate ārya āgacchannapi śobhate | [LalVis, 12 92.1]
sthito vātha niṣaṇṇo vā āryaḥ sarvatra śobhate | [LalVis, 12 92.2]
kathayaṃ śobhate āryastūṣṇībhūto 'pi śobhate | [LalVis, 12 93.1]
kalaviṅko yathā pakṣī darśanena svareṇa vā | [LalVis, 12 93.2]
kuśacīranivasto vā mandacailaḥ kṛśaṃtanuḥ | [LalVis, 12 94.1]
śobhate 'sau svatejena guṇavān guṇabhūṣitaḥ | [LalVis, 12 94.2]
sarveṇa śobhate āryo yasya pāpaṃ na vidyate | [LalVis, 12 95.1]
kiyadvibhūṣito bālaḥ pāpacārī na śobhate | [LalVis, 12 95.2]
ye kilbiṣāḥ svahṛdaye madhurāsu vācaṃ kumbho viṣasmi pariṣiktu yathāmṛtena | [LalVis, 12 96.1]
dusparśa śailaśilavat kaṭhināntarātmā sarpasya vā virasu darśana tādṛśānām | [LalVis, 12 96.2]
sarveṣu te namiṣu sarvamupaiti saumyāḥ sarveṣu tirthamiva sarvagopajīvyāḥ | [LalVis, 12 97.1]
dadhikṣīrapūrṇaghaṭatulya sadaiva āryā śuddhātmadarśanu sumaṅgalu tādṛśānām | [LalVis, 12 97.2]
yaiḥ pāpamitra parivarjita dīrgharātraṃ kalyāṇamitraratanaiśca parigṛhītāḥ | [LalVis, 12 98.1]
pāpaṃ vivarjayi niveśayi buddhadharme saphalaṃ sumaṅgalu sudarśanu tādṛśānām | [LalVis, 12 98.2]
ye kāyasaṃvṛta susaṃvṛtakāyadoṣāḥ ye vācasaṃvṛta sadānavakīrṇavācaḥ | [LalVis, 12 99.1]
guptendriyā sunibhṛtāśca manaḥprasannāḥ kiṃ tādṛśāna vadanaṃ pratichādayitvā | [LalVis, 12 99.2]
vastrā sahasra yadi chādayi ātmabhāvaṃ cittaṃ ca yeṣu vivṛtaṃ na hirī na lajjā | [LalVis, 12 100.1]
na ca yeṣu īdṛśa guṇā napi satyavākyaṃ nagne vinagnatara te vicaranti loke | [LalVis, 12 100.2]
yāścittagupta satatendriyasaṃyatāśca na ca anyasattvamanasā svapatīna tuṣṭāḥ | [LalVis, 12 101.1]
ādityacandrasadṛśā vivṛtaprakāśā kiṃ tādṛśāna vadanaṃ pratichādayitvā | [LalVis, 12 101.2]
api ca | [LalVis, 12 102.1]
jānanti āśayu mama ṛṣayo mahātmā paracittabuddhikuśalāstatha devasaṃghāḥ | [LalVis, 12 103.1]
yatha mahya śīlaguṇasaṃvaru apramādo vadanāvaguṇṭhanamataḥ prakaromi kiṃ me | [LalVis, 12 103.2]
aśrauṣīdbhikṣavo rājā śuddhodano nāma gopāyāḥ śākyakanyāyā imāmevaṃrūpāṃ sarvāṃ gāthāṃ pratibhānanirdeśam | [LalVis, 12 104.1]
śrutvā ca punastuṣṭa udagra āttamanāḥ pramuditaḥ prītisaumanasyajāto 'nekaratnapratyuptena dūṣyayugena koṭīśatasahasramūlyena ca muktāhāreṇābhijātalohitamuktāpratyuptayā ca suvarṇamālayā gopāṃ śākyakanyām abhicchādyainamudānamudānayati sma | [LalVis, 12 104.2]
yathā ca putro mama bhūṣito guṇais tathā ca kanyā svaguṇā prabhāsate | [LalVis, 12 105.1]
viśuddhasattvau tadubhau samāgatau sameti sarpir yatha sarpimaṇḍe | [LalVis, 12 105.2]
{LalVis, 13}
iti hi bhikṣava ātmarutaharṣamudīrayanta āgatā āsan bodhisattvasyāntaḥpuramadhyagatasya anekairdevair nāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragaśakrabrahmalokapālāḥ ye bodhisattvasya pūjākarmaṇe autsukyamāpatsyante sma | [LalVis, 13 1.1]
tatra bhikṣavo apareṇa samayena saṃbahulānāṃ devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragaśakrabrahmalokapālānām etadabhavad aticiraṃ batāyaṃ satpuruṣo 'ntaḥpure vilambitaḥ | [LalVis, 13 2.1]
ye cāsyeme dīrgharātraṃ paripācitāḥ sattvāścaturbhiḥ saṃgrahavastubhirdānena priyavākyenārthakriyayā samānārthatayā yasya bodhiprāptasya dharmadeśitamājñāsyanti tatsahaiva ca tāni dharmabhājanāni sarvāṇyantarhitāni bhaviṣyanti | [LalVis, 13 2.2]
bodhisattvaśca paścādabhiniṣkramyānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate | [LalVis, 13 2.3]
tataste sagauravāḥ sapratīkṣāḥ prāñjalībhūtā bodhisattvaṃ namasyanti sma | [LalVis, 13 3.1]
evamabhiprāyāścodīkṣamāṇāḥ sthitā abhūvan kadā ca nāma tadbhaviṣyati yadvayaṃ varapravaraṃ śuddhasattvamabhiniṣkrāmantaṃ paśyema abhiniṣkramya ca tasmin mahādrumarājamūle 'bhiniṣadya sabalaṃ māraṃ dharṣayitvā anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddhaṃ daśabhistathāgatabalaiḥ samanvāgataṃ caturbhiśca tathāgatavaiśāradyaiḥ samanvāgatamaṣṭādaśabhiścāveṇikairbuddhadharmaiḥ samanvāgataṃ triparivartaṃ dvādaśākāramanuttaraṃ dharmacakraṃ pravartayantaṃ mahatā buddhavikrīḍitena sadevamānuṣāsuralokaṃ yathādhimuktyā subhāṣitena saṃtoṣayantamiti | [LalVis, 13 3.2]
tatra bhikṣavo bodhisattvo dīrgharātramasaṃkhyeyān kalpānupādāya satataṃ samitamaparapraṇeyo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 13 4.1]
sarvalaukikalokottareṣu dharmeṣu svayamevācāryaḥ sarvakuśalamūladharmacaryāsu dīrghakālaṃ ca kālajño velājñaḥ samayajño 'bhūdacyuto 'bhijñaḥ pañcābhijñābhiḥ samanvāgato 'bhūt | [LalVis, 13 4.2]
ṛddhipādavikrīḍataḥ sarvendriyakuśalaḥ kālākālajñaḥ kālaveṣī mahāsāgara iva prāptāṃ velāṃ nātikrāmati sma | [LalVis, 13 4.3]
so 'bhijñajñānabalena samanvāgataḥ svayameva sarvaṃ jānāti sma | [LalVis, 13 4.4]
asyāyaṃ kālaḥ pragrahasya ayaṃ kālo nigrahasya ayaṃ kālaḥ saṃgrahasya ayaṃ kālo 'nugrahasya ayaṃ kāla upekṣāyā ayaṃ kālo bhāṣitasya ayaṃ kālastūṣṇīṃbhāvasya ayaṃ kālo niṣkramyasya ayaṃ kālaḥ pravrajyāyā ayaṃ kālaḥ svādhyāyasya ayaṃ kālo yoniśomanaskārasya ayaṃ kālaḥ pravivekasya ayaṃ kālaḥ kṣatriyaparṣadamupasaṃkramituṃ ............. peyālaṃ ............... yāvadayaṃ kālo brāhmaṇagṛhapatiparṣadamupasaṃkramitum ayaṃ kālo devanāgayakṣagandharvāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragaśakrabrahmalokapālabhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikāparṣadam upasaṃkramitum ayaṃ kālo dharmadeśanāyā ayaṃ kālaḥ pratisaṃlayanasya | [LalVis, 13 4.5]
sarvatra bodhisattvo nityakālaṃ kālajño bhavati sma kālaveṣī | [LalVis, 13 4.6]
atha ca punarbhikṣavo dharmatāpratilambha eṣa ca caramabhāvikānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ yadavaśyaṃ daśadiglokadhātusthitairbuddhair bhagavadbhirantaḥpuramadhyagatāḥ saṃgītitūryanirnāditairebhirevaṃrūpairdharmamukhaiḥ saṃcoditavyā bhavanti | [LalVis, 13 5.1]
tatredamucyate | [LalVis, 13 6.1]
bodhisattvasya khalu punarbhikṣavastasmin gṛhavarapradhāne sarvopakaraṇasamṛddhisamudite yathābhiprāyasukhavihārānukūle amarapurabhavanaprakāśe vitardiniryūhatoraṇagavākṣaharmyakūṭāgāraprāsādavarapravare sarvaratnavicitrālaṃkāravividhabhaktisuvibhakte ucchritachatradhvajapatākānekaratnakiṅkiṇījālasamalaṃkṛte anekapaṭṭadāmaśatasahasrābhipralambite nānāratnapratyupte muktāhārābhipralambite vicitrapaṭṭaratnasaṃkramopaśobhite avasaktapaṭṭamālyadāmakalāpe gandhaghaṭikānirdhūpite avaśyāyapaṭavitatavitāne sarvartukapuṣpaparamasugandhisurucirābhiprakīrṇapuṣkariṇīpuṇḍarīkanavanalinījālasaṃsthānaparibhogabahule patraguptaśukasārikakokilahaṃsamayūracakravākakunālakalaviṅkajīvajīvakādinānāvidhadvijagaṇamadhurasvaranikūjite nīlavaiḍūryamaye dharaṇītalasaṃsthānaparibhoge sarvarūpapratibhāsasaṃdarśane atṛptanayanābhiramye paramaprītiprāmodyasaṃjanane tasmin gṛhavarapradhāne 'dhyāvasato bodhisattvasyodāravaraśaraṇabhavananivāsino 'malavimalanirmalāṅgasyāmuktamālyābharaṇasya pravarasurabhigandhānulepanānuliptagātrasya śuklaśubhavimalaviśuddhanirmalavastraprāvṛtaśarīrasya anekadivyadūṣyasūkṣmasuvinyastamṛdukācilindikasukhasaṃsparśavarāṅgaracitaśayanatalābhirūḍhasya amaravadhūbhiriva sarvato 'navadyāpratikūladarśanaśubhopacāracaritasya abhirūpāntaḥpuramadhyagatasya śaṅkhabherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavatuṇavavīṇāvallakisaṃpatāḍakipalanakulasughoṣakamadhuraveṇunirnāditaghoṣarutanānātūryasaṃgītisaṃprayogapratibodhitasya ye ca nārīgaṇāḥ snigdhamadhuramanojñasvaraveṇunirnāditanirghoṣarutena bodhisattvaṃ pratisaṃbodhayanti sma teṣāṃ daśadigavasthitānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāmadhisthānena tebhyo veṇutūryaninādanirghoṣarutebhya imā bodhisattvasya saṃcodanā gāthā niścaranti sma | [LalVis, 13 15.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo 'ntaḥpuramadhyagato bodhisattvo 'virahito 'bhūddharmaśravaṇena avirahito 'bhūddharmamanasikāreṇa | [LalVis, 13 141.1]
tatkasmāddhetos tathā hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo dīrgharātraṃ sagauravo 'bhūt | [LalVis, 13 141.2]
dharmeṣu dharmabhāṇakeṣu cādhyāśayena dharmārthiko dharmakāmo dharmaratirato 'bhūt | [LalVis, 13 141.3]
dharmaparyeṣṭyatṛpto yathāśrutadharmasaṃprakāśakaḥ anuttaro mahādharmadānapatiḥ nirāmiṣadharmadeśako dharmadānenāmatsaraḥ ācāryamuṣṭivigato dharmānudharmapratipanno dharmapratipattiśūraḥ dharmalayano dharmatrāṇo dharmaśaraṇo dharmapratiśaraṇo dharmaparāyaṇaḥ dharmanidhyāptiḥ kṣāntiniryātaḥ prajñāpāramitācarita upāyakauśalyagatiṃ gataḥ | [LalVis, 13 141.4]
tatra bhikṣavo bodhisattvo mahopāyakauśalyavikrīḍitena sarvāntaḥpurasya yathādhimuktyā īryāpathamupadarśya paurvikāṇāṃ ca bodhisattvānāṃ lokaviṣayasamatikrāntānāṃ lokānuvartanakriyādharmatāmanuvartya dīrgharātraṃ suviditakāmadoṣaḥ sattvaparipākavaśād akāmāt kāmopabhogaṃ saṃdarśya aparimitakuśalamūlopacayapuṇyasaṃbhārabalaviśeṣaṇāsadṛśīṃ lokādhipateyatāṃ saṃdarśya devamanuṣyātikrāntaṃ sārodāravividhavicitrarūpaśabdagandharasasparśaparamaratiramaṇīyaṃ kāmaratirasaukhyamupadarśya sarvakāmaratisvaviṣayeṣvaparyantatvāt svacittavaśavartitāṃ saṃdarśya pūrvapraṇidhānabalasahāyakuśalamūlopacitān sattvān samānasaṃvāsatayā paripācya sarvalokasaṃkleśamalāsaṃkliṣṭacittatayāntaḥpuramadhyagato yathābhinimantritasya sattvadhātoḥ paripākakālamavekṣamāṇo bhūyasyā mātrayā bodhisattvastasmin samaye pūrvapratijñāmanusmarati sma buddhadharmāṃścāmukhīkaroti sma praṇidhānabalaṃ cābhinirharati sma | [LalVis, 13 142.1]
sattveṣu ca mahākaruṇāmavakrāmati sma | [LalVis, 13 142.2]
sattvapramokṣaṃ ca cintayati sma | [LalVis, 13 142.3]
sarvasaṃpado vipattiparyavasānā iti pratyavekṣate sma | [LalVis, 13 142.4]
anekopadravabhayabahulaṃ ca saṃsāramupaparīkṣate sma | [LalVis, 13 142.5]
mārakalipāśāṃśca saṃchinatti sma | [LalVis, 13 142.6]
saṃsāraprabandhāccātmānamuccārayati sma | [LalVis, 13 142.7]
nirvāṇe ca cittaṃ saṃpreṣayati sma | [LalVis, 13 142.8]
tatra bhikṣavo bodhisattvaḥ pūrvāntata eva suviditasaṃsāradoṣaḥ saṃskṛtenādhyāśayenānarthikaḥ sarvopādānaparigrahairanarthiko buddhadharmanirvāṇābhimukhaḥ saṃsāraparāṅmukhastathāgatagocarābhirataḥ māraviṣayagocarāsaṃsṛṣṭaḥ ādīptabhavadoṣadarśī traidhātukānniḥśaraṇābhiprāyaḥ saṃsāradoṣādīnavaniḥsaraṇakuśalaḥ pravrajyābhilāṣī niṣkramaṇābhiprāyo vivekanimno vivekapravaṇo vivekaprāgbhāraḥ āraṇyaprāraṇyābhimukhaḥ pravivekapraśamābhikāṅkṣī ātmaparahitapratipannaḥ anuttarapratipattiśūro lokasyārthakāmo hitakāmaḥ sukhakāmo yogakṣemakāmo lokānukampako hitaiṣī maitrīvihārī mahākāruṇikaḥ saṃgrahavastukuśalaḥ satatasamitam aparikhinnamānasaḥ sattvaparipākavinayakuśalaḥ sarvasattveṣvekaputrakapremānugatamanasikāraḥ sarvavastunirapekṣaparityāgī dānasaṃvibhāgarataḥ prayuktatyāgaḥ prayatapāṇiḥ tyāgaśūro yaṣṭayajñaḥ susamṛddhapuṇyaḥ susaṃgṛhītapuṇyaḥ pariṣkāravigatamalāmātsaryasunigṛhītacitto 'nuttaro mahādānapatirdattvā ca vipākāpratikāṅkṣī pradānaśūraḥ icchāmahecchālobhadveṣamadamānamohamātsaryapramukhasarvārikleśagaṇapratyarthikanigrahāyābhyutthitaḥ sarvajñatācittotpādaprabandhāccalitaḥ mahātyāgacittasaṃnāhasusaṃnaddhaḥ lokānukampako hitaiṣīva varmitakavacitavīryaḥ sattvapramokṣālambanamahākaruṇābalavikramaparākramaḥ avaivartikasarvasattvasamacittatyāgapraharaṇo yathābhiprāyasattvāśayasaṃtoṣaṇo bodhibhājanībhūtaḥ kālākṣuṇṇadharmavedhī bodhipariṇāmapraṇidhiḥ anavanāmitadhvajas trimaṇḍalapariśodhanadānaparityāgī jñānavaravajradṛḍhapraharaṇaḥ sunigṛhītakleśapratyarthikaḥ śīlaguṇacāritrapratipannaḥ svārakṣitakāyavāṅmanaskarmānto 'ṇumātrāvadyabhayadarśī supariśuddhaśīlaḥ amalavimalanirmalacittaḥ sarvaduruktadurāgatavacanapathākrośaparibhāṣaṇakutsanatāḍanatarjanavadhabandhanāvarodhanaparikleśāluḍitacitto 'kṣubhitacittaḥ kṣāntisaurabhyasampannaḥ akṣato 'nupahato 'vyāpannacittaḥ sarvasattvahitārthāyottaptavīryārambhī dṛḍhasamādānasarvakuśalamūladharmasamudānayanāpratyudāvartyasmṛtimān susaṃprajñāsusamāhito 'vikṣiptacitto dhyānaikāgramanasikāro dharmapravicayakuśalo labdhāloko vigatatamo'ndhakāraḥ anityaduḥkhātmāśubhākāraparibhāvitacetāḥ smṛtyupasthānasamyakprahāṇaṛddhipādendriyabalabodhyaṅgamārgāryasatyasarvabodhipakṣadharmasuparikarmakṛtamanasikāraḥ śamathavipaśyanāsuparyavadātabuddhiḥ pratītyasamutpādasatyadarśī satyānubodhādaparapratyayastrivimokṣasukhavikrīḍito māyāmarīcisvapnodakacandrapratiśrutkāpratibhāsopamasarvadharmanayāvatīrṇaḥ | [LalVis, 13 143.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvasyaivaṃ bhavati pratikṛtiḥ evaṃ dharmavihārī evaṃ guṇamāhātmyavihārī evaṃ sattvārthābhiyuktavihārī abhūt | [LalVis, 13 144.1]
bhūyasyā mātrayā ābhirdaśadigbuddhādhiṣṭhānatūryasaṃgītiviniḥsṛtābhirgāthābhiḥ saṃcoditaḥ sa tasyāṃ velāyāṃ pūrveṣāṃ ca bodhisattvānāṃ caramabhavopagatānām antaḥpuraparipācitāni catvāri dharmamukhānyāmukhīkaroti sma | [LalVis, 13 144.2]
katamāni catvāri yadidaṃ dānaṃ priyavacanamarthakriyāṃ samānārthatāṃ ca | [LalVis, 13 144.3]
catuḥsaṃgrahavastuprayoganirhāraviśuddhiṃ ca nāma dharmamukhamāmukhīkaroti sma | [LalVis, 13 144.4]
triratnavaṃśasādhāraṇābhiprāyo vipraṇāśasarvajñatācittapraṇidhānabalādhānāvaivartyaviṣayaṃ ca nāma dharmamukhamāmukhīkaroti sma | [LalVis, 13 144.5]
sarvasattvāparityāgādhyāśayamahākaruṇāvatāratāṃ ca nāma dharmamukhamāmukhīkaroti sma | [LalVis, 13 144.6]
sarvabodhipakṣadharmapade prabhedārthābhiniścayajñānasaṃsārabalaviśeṣasamudānayamahāvyūhaṃ ca nāma dharmamukhamāmukhīkaroti sma | [LalVis, 13 144.7]
imāni catvāri dharmamukhānyāmukhīkṛtya bodhisattvaḥ sarvasyāntaḥpurasya paripācanārthaṃ tasyāṃ velāyāṃ tathārūpamṛddhyabhisaṃskāramabhisaṃskaroti sma yathārūpeṇa ṛddhyabhisaṃskāreṇābhisaṃskṛtena tebhyaḥ saṃgītirutebhyo bodhisattvānubhāvenemānyevaṃrūpāṇi dharmamukhaśatasahasrāṇi niścaranti sma | [LalVis, 13 144.8]
tadyathā | [LalVis, 13 144.9]
iti hi bhikṣavo 'ntaḥpuramadhyagatena bodhisattvena tāni caturaśītistrīsahasrāṇi paripācitānyabhūvan anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau bahūni ca devatāśatasahasrāṇi ye tatra samprāptā abhūvan | [LalVis, 13 153.1]
tathā abhiniṣkramaṇakāle tasmin samaye bodhisattvasya hrīdevo nāma tuṣitakāyiko devaputro 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ sa rātrau praśāntāyāṃ dvātriṃśatā devaputrasahasraiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛto yena bodhisattvasyopasthānaprāsādas tenopasaṃkrāmat | [LalVis, 13 154.1]
upasaṃkramya gaganatalagata eva bodhisattvaṃ gāthābhiradhyabhāṣata | [LalVis, 13 154.2]
{LalVis, 14}
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvaḥ saṃcoditaḥ san tena devaputreṇa rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyemaṃ svapnamupadarśayati sma yadrājā śuddhodanaḥ suptaḥ svapnāntaragato 'drākṣīt bodhisattvaṃ rātrau praśāntāyāmabhiniṣkramantaṃ devagaṇaparivṛtam | [LalVis, 14 1.1]
abhiniṣkramya pravrajitaṃ cādrākṣīt kāṣāyavastraprāvṛtam | [LalVis, 14 1.2]
sa pratibuddhaḥ tvaritaṃ tvaritaṃ kāñcukīyaṃ paripṛcchati sma kaccit kumāro 'ntaḥpure 'sti so 'vocat asti deveti | [LalVis, 14 1.3]
tato rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyāntaḥpure śokaśalyo hṛdaye 'nupraviṣṭo 'bhūd abhiniṣkramiṣyati avaśyaṃ kumāro 'yam | [LalVis, 14 2.1]
yaccemāni pūrvanimittāni saṃdṛśyante sma | [LalVis, 14 2.2]
tasyaitadabhavan na khalvavyayaṃ kumāreṇa kadācidudyānabhūmimabhinirgantavyam | [LalVis, 14 3.1]
strīgaṇamadhye 'bhirataḥ ihaiva ramyate nābhiniṣkramiṣyatīti | [LalVis, 14 3.2]
tato rājñā śuddhodanena kumārasya paribhogārthaṃ trayo yathartukāḥ prāsādāḥ kāritā abhūvan graiṣmiko vārṣiko haimantikaśca | [LalVis, 14 4.1]
tatra yo graiṣmikaḥ sa ekāntaśītalaḥ | [LalVis, 14 4.2]
yo vārṣikaḥ sa sādhāraṇaḥ | [LalVis, 14 4.3]
yo haimantikaḥ sa svabhāvoṣṇaḥ | [LalVis, 14 4.4]
ekaikasya ca prāsādasya sopānāni pañca pañca puruṣaśatānyutkṣipanti sma nikṣipanti sma | [LalVis, 14 4.5]
teṣāṃ tathotkṣipyamāṇānāṃ nikṣipyamāṇānāṃ ca śabdo 'rdhayojane śrūyate sma mā khalu kumāro 'nabhijñāta evābhiniṣkramiṣyatīti | [LalVis, 14 4.6]
naimittikairvaipañcikaiśca vyākṛtamabhūn maṅgaladvāreṇa kumāro 'bhiniṣkramiṣyatīti | [LalVis, 14 4.7]
tato rājā maṅgaladvārasya mahānti kapāṭāni kārayati sma | [LalVis, 14 4.8]
ekaikaṃ ca kapāṭaṃ pañca pañca puruṣaśatānyudghāṭayanti sma apaghāṭayanti sma | [LalVis, 14 4.9]
teṣāṃ cārdhayojanaṃ śabdo gacchati sma | [LalVis, 14 4.10]
pañca cāsya kāmaguṇān sadṛśānupasaṃharati sma | [LalVis, 14 4.11]
gītavāditanṛtyaiścainaṃ sadaiva yuvataya upatasthuḥ | [LalVis, 14 4.12]
atha bhikṣavo bodhisattvaḥ sārathiṃ prāha śīghraṃ sārathe rathaṃ yojaya | [LalVis, 14 5.1]
udyānabhūmiṃ gamiṣyāmīti | [LalVis, 14 5.2]
tataḥ sārathī rājānaṃ śuddhodanam upasaṃkramyaivamāha deva kumāra udyānabhūmimabhiniryāsyatīti | [LalVis, 14 5.3]
atha rājñaḥ śuddhodanasyaitadabhavan na kadācinmayā kumāra udyānabhūmimabhiniṣkramitaḥ subhūmidarśanāya | [LalVis, 14 6.1]
yannvahaṃ kumāramudyānabhūmimabhiniṣkrāmayeyam | [LalVis, 14 6.2]
tataḥ kumāraḥ strīgaṇaparivṛto ratiṃ vetsyate nābhiniṣkramiṣyatīti | [LalVis, 14 6.3]
tato rājā śuddhodanaḥ snehabahumānābhyāṃ bodhisattvasya nagare ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇāṃ kārayati sma saptame divase kumāra udyānabhūmiṃ niṣkramiṣyatīti subhūmidarśanāya | [LalVis, 14 7.1]
tatra bhavadbhiḥ sarvāmanāpāni cāpanayitavyāni mā kumāraḥ pratikūlaṃ paśyet | [LalVis, 14 7.2]
sarvamanāpāni copasaṃhartavyāni viṣayābhiramyāṇi | [LalVis, 14 7.3]
tataḥ saptame divase sarvaṃ nagaramalaṃkṛtamabhūd udyānabhūmimupaśobhitaṃ nānāraṅgadūṣyavitānīkṛtaṃ chatradhvajapatākāsamalaṃkṛtam | [LalVis, 14 8.1]
yena ca mārgeṇa bodhisattvo 'bhinirgacchati sma sa mārgaḥ siktaḥ saṃmṛṣṭo gandhodakapariṣikto muktakusumāvakīrṇo nānāgandhaghaṭikānirdhūpitaḥ pūrṇakumbhopaśobhitaḥ kadalīvṛkṣocchrito nānāvicitrapaṭavitānavitato ratnakiṅkiṇījālahārārdhahārābhipralambito 'bhūt | [LalVis, 14 8.2]
caturaṅgasainyavyūhitaḥ parivāraścodyukto 'bhūt kumārasyāntaḥpuraṃ pratimaṇḍayitum | [LalVis, 14 8.3]
atha śuddhāvāsakāyikā devā nidhyāpayanti sma bodhisattvamāharitum tatra bodhisattvasya pūrveṇa nagaradvāreṇodyānabhūmimabhiniṣkrāmato mahatā vyūhena atha bodhisattvasyānubhāvena śuddhavāsakāyikair devaputraistasmin mārge puruṣo jīrṇo vṛddho mahallako dhamanīsaṃtatagātraḥ khaṇḍadanto valīnicitakāyaḥ palitakeśaḥ kubjo gopānasīvakro vibhagno daṇḍaparāyaṇa āturo gatayauvanaḥ kharakharāvasaktakaṇṭhaḥ prāgbhāreṇa kāyena daṇḍamavaṣṭabhya pravepayamānaḥ sarvāṅgapratyaṅgaiḥ purato mārgasyopadarśito 'bhūt | [LalVis, 14 8.4]
atha bodhisattvo jānanneva sārathimidamavocat | [LalVis, 14 9.1]
kiṃ sārathe puruṣa durbala alpasthāmo ucchuṣkamāṃsarudhiratvacasnāyunaddhaḥ | [LalVis, 14 10.1]
śvetaṃśiro viraladanta kṛśāṅgarūpo ālambya daṇḍa vrajate asukhaṃ skhalantaḥ | [LalVis, 14 10.2]
sārathirāha | [LalVis, 14 11.1]
atha bodhisattvaḥ pratinivartya rathavaraṃ punarapi puraṃ prāviśat | [LalVis, 14 19.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo 'pareṇa kālasamayena dakṣiṇena nagaradvāreṇodyānabhūmimabhiniṣkraman mahatā vyūhena so 'drākṣīnmārge puruṣaṃ vyādhispṛṣṭaṃ dagdhodarābhibhūtaṃ durbalakāyaṃ svake mūtrapurīṣe nimagnam atrāṇam apratiśaraṇaṃ kṛcchreṇocchvasantaṃ praśvasantam | [LalVis, 14 20.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarbodhisattvo jānanneva sārathimidamavocat | [LalVis, 14 20.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavo bodhisattvaḥ pratinivartya rathavaraṃ punarapi puravaraṃ prāvikṣat | [LalVis, 14 26.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvo 'pareṇa kālasamayena paścimena nagaradvāreṇodyānabhūmimabhiniṣkraman mahatā vyūhena so 'drākṣīt puruṣaṃ mṛtaṃ kālagataṃ mañce samāropitaṃ cailavitānīkṛtaṃ jñātisaṃghaparivṛtaṃ sarvai rudadbhiḥ krandadbhiḥ paridevamānaiḥ prakīrṇakeśaiḥ pāṃśvavakīrṇaśirobhirurāṃsi tāḍayadbhirutkrośadbhiḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nugacchadbhiḥ | [LalVis, 14 27.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarbodhisattvo jānanneva sārathimidamavocat | [LalVis, 14 27.2]
atha khalu bhikṣavo bodhisattvaḥ pratinivartya taṃ rathavaraṃ punarapi puraṃ prāvikṣat | [LalVis, 14 34.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo bodhisattvasyāpareṇa kālasamayenottareṇa nagaradvāreṇodyānabhūmim abhiniṣkrāmatastaireva devaputrairbodhisattvasyānubhāvenaiva tasminmārge bhikṣurabhinirmito 'bhūt | [LalVis, 14 35.1]
adrākṣīdbodhisattvastaṃ bhikṣuṃ śāntaṃ dāntaṃ saṃyataṃ brahmacāriṇam avikṣiptacakṣuṣaṃ yugamātraprekṣiṇaṃ prāsādikenairyāpathena sampannaṃ prāsādikenābhikramapratikrameṇa sampannaṃ prāsādikenāvalokitavyavalokitena prāsādikena samiñjitaprasāritena prāsādikena saṃghāṭīpātracīvaradhāraṇena mārge sthitam | [LalVis, 14 35.2]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarbodhisattvo jānanneva sārathimidamavocat | [LalVis, 14 35.3]
atha khalu bhikṣavo bodhisattvaḥ pratinivartya taṃ rathavaraṃ punarapi puravaraṃ prāvikṣat | [LalVis, 14 41.1]
iti hi bhikṣavo rājā śuddhodano bodhisattvasyemāmevaṃrūpāṃ saṃcodanāṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca bhūyasyā mātrayā bodhisattvasya parirakṣaṇārthaṃ prākārān māpayate sma parikhāḥ khānayati sma dvārāṇi ca gāḍhāni kārayati sma | [LalVis, 14 42.1]
ārakṣān sthāpayati sma | [LalVis, 14 42.2]
śūrāṃścodayati sma | [LalVis, 14 42.3]
vāhanāni yojayati sma | [LalVis, 14 42.4]
varmāṇi grāhayati sma | [LalVis, 14 42.5]
caturṣu nagaradvāraśṛṅgāṭakeṣu caturo mahāsenāvyūhān sthāpayati sma bodhisattvasya parirakṣaṇārtham | [LalVis, 14 42.6]
ya enaṃ rātriṃdivaṃ rakṣanti sma mā bodhisattvo 'bhiniṣkramiṣyatīti | [LalVis, 14 42.7]
antaḥpure cājñāṃ dadāti sma mā sma kadācitsaṃgītiṃ vicchetsyatha | [LalVis, 14 42.8]
sarvaratikrīḍāścopasaṃhartavyāḥ strīmāyāścopadarśayata nirbandhata kumāraṃ yathānuraktacitto na nirgacchetpravrajyāyai | [LalVis, 14 42.9]
